Itletay: Omeoray anday Ulietjay

Authoray: Illiamway Akespeareshay

Eleaseray ateday: Ovembernay 1ay, 199ay8 ebOok[ay #1513ay]
Ostmay ecentlyray updateday: Eptembersay 18ay, 202ay5

Anguagelay: Englishay

Editscray: ethay Pgay Akespeareshay Eamtay, aay eamtay ofay aboutay entytway Ojectpray Utenberggay olunteersvay


**ay* ARTStay Ofay EThay OJECTPray UTENBERGgay EBOOkay OMEOray ANday ULIETjay **ay*




EThay AGEDYTray Ofay OMEOray ANday ULIETjay

byay Illiamway Akespeareshay




Ontentscay

EThay OLOGUEPray.

ACtay Iay
Enescay Iay. Aay ublicpay aceplay.
Enescay Iiay. Aay Eetstray.
Enescay IIiay. Oomray inay Apulet’scay Ousehay.
Enescay Ivay. Aay Eetstray.
Enescay Vay. Aay Allhay inay Apulet’scay Ousehay.

ACtay Iiay
ORUSChay.
Enescay Iay. Anay openay aceplay adjoiningay Apulet’scay Ardengay.
Enescay Iiay. Apulet’scay Ardengay.
Enescay IIiay. Iarfray Awrence’slay Ellcay.
Enescay Ivay. Aay Eetstray.
Enescay Vay. Apulet’scay Ardengay.
Enescay Ivay. Iarfray Awrence’slay Ellcay.

ACtay IIiay
Enescay Iay. Aay ublicpay Aceplay.
Enescay Iiay. Aay Oomray inay Apulet’scay Ousehay.
Enescay IIiay. Iarfray Awrence’slay ellcay.
Enescay Ivay. Aay Oomray inay Apulet’scay Ousehay.
Enescay Vay. Anay openay Allerygay otay Uliet’sjay Amberchay, overlookingay ethay Ardengay.

ACtay Ivay
Enescay Iay. Iarfray Awrence’slay Ellcay.
Enescay Iiay. Allhay inay Apulet’scay Ousehay.
Enescay IIiay. Uliet’sjay Amberchay.
Enescay Ivay. Allhay inay Apulet’scay Ousehay.
Enescay Vay. Uliet’sjay Amberchay; Ulietjay onay ethay edbay.

ACtay Vay
Enescay Iay. Antuamay. Aay Eetstray.
Enescay Iiay. Iarfray Awrence’slay Ellcay.
Enescay IIiay. Aay urchyardchay; inay itay aay Onumentmay elongingbay otay ethay Apuletscay.




Amatisdray Ersonæpay

ESCALUsay, Incepray ofay Eronavay.
ERCUTIOmay, insmankay otay ethay Incepray, anday iendfray otay Omeoray.
ARISpay, aay oungyay Oblemannay, insmankay otay ethay Incepray.
Agepay otay Arispay.

ONTAGUEmay, eadhay ofay aay Eronesevay amilyfay atay eudfay ithway ethay Apuletscay.
ADYlay ONTAGUEmay, ifeway otay Ontaguemay.
OMEOray, onsay otay Ontaguemay.
ENVOLIObay, ephewnay otay Ontaguemay, anday iendfray otay Omeoray.
ABRAmay, ervantsay otay Ontaguemay.
ALTHASARbay, ervantsay otay Omeoray.

APULETcay, eadhay ofay aay Eronesevay amilyfay atay eudfay ithway ethay Ontaguesmay.
ADYlay APULETcay, ifeway otay Apuletcay.
ULIETjay, aughterday otay Apuletcay.
ALTTYbay, ephewnay otay Adylay Apuletcay.
APULET’scay OUSINcay, anay olday anmay.
URSEnay otay Ulietjay.
ETERpay, ervantsay otay Uliet’sjay Ursenay.
AMPSONsay, ervantsay otay Apuletcay.
EGORYGray, ervantsay otay Apuletcay.
Ervantssay.

IARFray AWRENCElay, aay Anciscanfray.
IARFray OHNjay, ofay ethay amesay Orderay.
Anay Apothecaryay.
ORUSChay.
Eethray Usiciansmay.
Anay Officeray.
Itizenscay ofay Eronavay; everalsay Enmay anday Omenway, elationsray otay othbay ouseshay;
Askersmay, Uardsgay, Atchmenway anday Attendantsay.

ENEScay. Uringday ethay eatergray artpay ofay ethay Ayplay inay Eronavay; onceay, inay ethay
Ifthfay Actay, atay Antuamay.




EThay OLOGUEPray


Enteray Oruschay.

ORUSChay.
Otway ouseholdshay, othbay alikeay inay ignityday,
Inay airfay Eronavay, erewhay eway aylay ouray enescay,
Omfray ancientay udgegray eakbray otay ewnay utinymay,
Erewhay ivilcay oodblay akesmay ivilcay andshay uncleanay.
Omfray orthfay ethay atalfay oinslay ofay esethay otway oesfay
Aay airpay ofay ar-cross’dstay overslay aketay eirthay ifelay;
Osewhay isadventur’dmay iteouspay overthrowsay
Othday ithway eirthay eathday urybay eirthay arentspay’ ifestray.
Ethay earfulfay assagepay ofay eirthay eath-mark’dday ovelay,
Anday ethay ontinuancecay ofay eirthay arentspay’ ageray,
Ichwhay, utbay eirthay ildren’schay enday, oughtnay ouldcay emoveray,
Isay ownay ethay otway ourshay’ affictray ofay ouray agestay;
Ethay ichwhay, ifay ouyay ithway atientpay earsay attenday,
Atwhay erehay allshay issmay, ouray oiltay allshay ivestray otay endmay.

exIt._[_ay]




ACtay Iay

ENEScay Iay. Aay ublicpay aceplay.


Enteray Ampsonsay anday Egorygray armeday ithway ordssway anday ucklersbay.

AMPSONsay.
Egorygray, onay myay ordway, e’llway otnay arrycay oalscay.

EGORYGray.
Onay, orfay enthay eway ouldshay ebay ollierscay.

AMPSONsay.
Iay eanmay, ifay eway ebay inay olerchay, e’llway awdray.

EGORYGray.
Ayay, ilewhay ouyay ivelay, awdray ouryay ecknay outay oay’ ethay ollarcay.

AMPSONsay.
Iay ikestray uicklyqay, eingbay ovedmay.

EGORYGray.
Utbay outhay artay otnay uicklyqay ovedmay otay ikestray.

AMPSONsay.
Aay ogday ofay ethay ousehay ofay Ontaguemay ovesmay emay.

EGORYGray.
Otay ovemay isay otay irstay; anday otay ebay aliantvay isay otay andstay: ereforethay, ifay outhay
artay ovedmay, outhay unn’stray awayay.

AMPSONsay.
Aay ogday ofay atthay ousehay allshay ovemay emay otay andstay.
Iay illway aketay ethay allway ofay anyay anmay oray aidmay ofay Ontague’smay.

EGORYGray.
Atthay owsshay eethay aay eakway aveslay, orfay ethay eakestway oesgay otay ethay allway.

AMPSONsay.
Uetray, anday ereforethay omenway, eingbay ethay eakerway esselsvay, areay everay ustthray otay
ethay allway: ereforethay Iay illway ushpay Ontague’smay enmay omfray ethay allway, anday
ustthray ishay aidsmay otay ethay allway.

EGORYGray.
Ethay uarrelqay isay etweenbay ouray astersmay anday usay eirthay enmay.

AMPSONsay.
iS’tay allay oneay, Iay illway owshay elfmysay aay anttyray: enwhay Iay avehay oughtfay ithway ethay
enmay Iay illway ebay ivilcay ithway ethay aidsmay, Iay illway utcay offay eirthay eadshay.

EGORYGray.
Ethay eadshay ofay ethay aidsmay?

AMPSONsay.
Ayay, ethay eadshay ofay ethay aidsmay, oray eirthay aidenheadsmay; aketay itay inay atwhay ensesay
outhay iltway.

EGORYGray.
Eythay ustmay aketay itay inay ensesay atthay eelfay itay.

AMPSONsay.
Emay eythay allshay eelfay ilewhay Iay amay ableay otay andstay: anday is’tay ownknay Iay amay aay
ettypray iecepay ofay eshflay.

EGORYGray.
iS’tay ellway outhay artay otnay ishfay; ifay outhay adsthay, outhay adsthay eenbay oorpay Ohnjay.
Awdray thyay ooltay; erehay omescay ofay ethay ousehay ofay Ontaguesmay.

Enteray Abramay anday Althasarbay.

AMPSONsay.
Myay akednay eaponway isay outay: uarrelqay, Iay illway ackbay eethay.

EGORYGray.
Owhay? Urntay thyay ackbay anday unray?

AMPSONsay.
Earfay emay otnay.

EGORYGray.
Onay, arrymay; Iay earfay eethay!

AMPSONsay.
Etlay usay aketay ethay awlay ofay ouray idessay; etlay emthay eginbay.

EGORYGray.
Iay illway ownfray asay Iay asspay byay, anday etlay emthay aketay itay asay eythay istlay.

AMPSONsay.
Aynay, asay eythay areday. Iay illway itebay myay umbthay atay emthay, ichwhay isay isgraceday otay
emthay ifay eythay earbay itay.

ABRAmay.
Oday ouyay itebay ouryay umbthay atay usay, irsay?

AMPSONsay.
Iay oday itebay myay umbthay, irsay.

ABRAmay.
Oday ouyay itebay ouryay umbthay atay usay, irsay?

AMPSONsay.
Isay ethay awlay ofay ouray idesay ifay Iay aysay ayay?

EGORYGray.
Onay.

AMPSONsay.
Onay irsay, Iay oday otnay itebay myay umbthay atay ouyay, irsay; utbay Iay itebay myay umbthay, irsay.

EGORYGray.
Oday ouyay uarrelqay, irsay?

ABRAmay.
Uarrelqay, irsay? Onay, irsay.

AMPSONsay.
Utbay ifay ouyay oday, irsay, Iay amay orfay ouyay. Iay ervesay asay oodgay aay anmay asay ouyay.

ABRAmay.
Onay etterbay.

AMPSONsay.
Ellway, irsay.

Enteray Envoliobay.

EGORYGray.
Aysay etterbay; erehay omescay oneay ofay myay aster’smay insmenkay.

AMPSONsay.
Esyay, etterbay, irsay.

ABRAmay.
Ouyay ielay.

AMPSONsay.
Awdray, ifay ouyay ebay enmay. Egorygray, ememberray thyay ashingway owblay.

ey[_thay ight._fay]

ENVOLIObay.
Artpay, oolsfay! utpay upay ouryay ordssway, ouyay owknay otnay atwhay ouyay oday.

eaTs[_bay ownday eirthay ords._sway]

Enteray Alttybay.

ALTTYbay.
Atwhay, artay outhay awndray amongay esethay eartlesshay indshay?
Urntay eethay Envoliobay, ooklay uponay thyay eathday.

ENVOLIObay.
Iay oday utbay eepkay ethay eacepay, utpay upay thyay ordsway,
Oray anagemay itay otay artpay esethay enmay ithway emay.

ALTTYbay.
Atwhay, awndray, anday alktay ofay eacepay? Iay atehay ethay ordway
Asay Iay atehay ellhay, allay Ontaguesmay, anday eethay:
Avehay atay eethay, owardcay.

ey[_thay ight._fay]

Enteray eethray oray ourfay Itizenscay ithway ubsclay.

IRSTfay ITIZENcay.
Ubsclay, illsbay anday artisanspay! Ikestray! Eatbay emthay ownday!
Ownday ithway ethay Apuletscay! Ownday ithway ethay Ontaguesmay!

Enteray Apuletcay inay ishay owngay, anday Adylay Apuletcay.

APULETcay.
Atwhay oisenay isay isthay? Ivegay emay myay onglay ordsway, ohay!

ADYlay APULETcay.
Aay utchcray, aay utchcray! Whyay allcay ouyay orfay aay ordsway?

APULETcay.
Myay ordsway, Iay aysay! Olday Ontaguemay isay omecay,
Anday ourishesflay ishay adeblay inay itespay ofay emay.

Enteray Ontaguemay anday ishay Adylay Ontaguemay.

ONTAGUEmay.
Outhay illainvay Apuletcay! Oldhay emay otnay, etlay emay ogay.

ADYlay ONTAGUEmay.
Outhay altshay otnay irstay oneay ootfay otay eeksay aay oefay.

Enteray Incepray Escalusay, ithway Attendantsay.

INCEPray.
Ebelliousray ubjectssay, enemiesay otay eacepay,
Ofanerspray ofay isthay eighbour-stainednay eel,stay—
Illway eythay otnay earhay? Atwhay, ohay! Ouyay enmay, ouyay eastsbay,
Atthay uenchqay ethay irefay ofay ouryay erniciouspay ageray
Ithway urplepay ountainsfay issuingay omfray ouryay einsvay,
Onay ainpay ofay orturetay, omfray osethay oodyblay andshay
Owthray ouryay istemper’dmay eaponsway otay ethay oundgray
Anday earhay ethay entencesay ofay ouryay ovedmay incepray.
Eethray ivilcay awlsbray, edbray ofay anay airyay ordway,
Byay eethay, olday Apuletcay, anday Ontaguemay,
Avehay icethray isturb’dday ethay uietqay ofay ouray eetsstray,
Anday ademay Erona’svay ancientay itizenscay
Astcay byay eirthay avegray eseemingbay ornamentsay,
Otay ieldway olday artisanspay, inay andshay asay olday,
Anker’dcay ithway eacepay, otay artpay ouryay anker’dcay atehay.
Ifay everay ouyay isturbday ouray eetsstray againay,
Ouryay iveslay allshay aypay ethay orfeitfay ofay ethay eacepay.
Orfay isthay imetay allay ethay estray epartday awayay:
Ouyay, Apuletcay, allshay ogay alongay ithway emay,
Anday Ontaguemay, omecay ouyay isthay afternoonay,
Otay owknay ouray artherfay easureplay inay isthay asecay,
Otay olday Ee-townfray, ouray ommoncay udgement-placejay.
Onceay oremay, onay ainpay ofay eathday, allay enmay epartday.

exEunt[_ay Incepray anday Attendantsay; Apuletcay, Adylay Apuletcay, Alttybay,
Itizenscay anday Ervants._say]

ONTAGUEmay.
Owhay etsay isthay ancientay uarrelqay ewnay abroachay?
Eakspay, ephewnay, ereway ouyay byay enwhay itay eganbay?

ENVOLIObay.
Erehay ereway ethay ervantssay ofay ouryay adversaryay
Anday oursyay, oseclay ightingfay ereay Iay idday approachay.
Iay ewdray otay artpay emthay, inay ethay instantay amecay
Ethay ieryfay Alttybay, ithway ishay ordsway epar’dpray,
Ichwhay, asay ehay eath’dbray efianceday otay myay earsay,
Ehay ungsway aboutay ishay eadhay, anday utcay ethay indsway,
Owhay othingnay urthay ithalway, iss’dhay imhay inay ornscay.
Ilewhay eway ereway interchangingay uststhray anday owsblay
Amecay oremay anday oremay, anday oughtfay onay artpay anday artpay,
Illtay ethay Incepray amecay, owhay artedpay eitheray artpay.

ADYlay ONTAGUEmay.
Oay erewhay isay Omeoray, awsay ouyay imhay odaytay?
Ightray adglay Iay amay ehay asway otnay atay isthay ayfray.

ENVOLIObay.
Adammay, anay ourhay eforebay ethay orshipp’dway unsay
Eer’dpay orthfay ethay oldengay indowway ofay ethay eastay,
Aay oubledtray indmay avedray emay otay alkway abroaday,
Erewhay underneathay ethay ovegray ofay amoresycay
Atthay estwardway ootethray omfray isthay itycay idesay,
Osay earlyay alkingway idday Iay eesay ouryay onsay.
Owardstay imhay Iay ademay, utbay ehay asway areway ofay emay,
Anday olestay intoay ethay overtcay ofay ethay oodway.
Iay, easuringmay ishay affectionsay byay myay ownay,
Ichwhay enthay ostmay oughtsay erewhay ostmay ightmay otnay ebay oundfay,
Eingbay oneay ootay anymay byay myay earyway elfsay,
Ursu’dpay myay umourhay, otnay ursuingpay ishay,
Anday adlyglay unn’dshay owhay adlyglay edflay omfray emay.

ONTAGUEmay.
Anymay aay orningmay athhay ehay erethay eenbay eensay,
Ithway earstay augmentingay ethay eshfray orning’smay ewday,
Addingay otay oudsclay oremay oudsclay ithway ishay eepday ighssay;
Utbay allay osay oonsay asay ethay all-cheeringay unsay
Ouldshay inay ethay arthestfay eastay eginbay otay awdray
Ethay adyshay urtainscay omfray Aurora’say edbay,
Awayay omfray ightlay ealsstay omehay myay eavyhay onsay,
Anday ivatepray inay ishay amberchay enspay imselfhay,
Utsshay upay ishay indowsway, ockslay airfay aylightday outay
Anday akesmay imselfhay anay artificialay ightnay.
Ackblay anday ortentouspay ustmay isthay umourhay ovepray,
Unlessay oodgay ounselcay aymay ethay ausecay emoveray.

ENVOLIObay.
Myay oblenay uncleay, oday ouyay owknay ethay ausecay?

ONTAGUEmay.
Iay eithernay owknay itay ornay ancay earnlay ofay imhay.

ENVOLIObay.
Avehay ouyay importun’day imhay byay anyay eansmay?

ONTAGUEmay.
Othbay byay elfmysay anday anymay otheray iendsfray;
Utbay ehay, ishay ownay affectionsay’ ounsellorcay,
Isay otay imself—ihay illway otnay aysay owhay uetray—
Utbay otay imselfhay osay ecretsay anday osay oseclay,
Osay arfay omfray oundingsay anday iscoveryday,
Asay isay ethay udbay itbay ithway anay enviousay ormway
Ereay ehay ancay eadspray ishay eetsway eaveslay otay ethay airay,
Oray edicateday ishay eautybay otay ethay unsay.
Ouldcay eway utbay earnlay omfray encewhay ishay orrowssay owgray,
Eway ouldway asay illinglyway ivegay urecay asay owknay.

Enteray Omeoray.

ENVOLIObay.
Eesay, erewhay ehay omescay. Osay easeplay ouyay epstay asideay;
I’llay owknay ishay ievancegray oray ebay uchmay eniedday.

ONTAGUEmay.
Iay ouldway outhay ertway osay appyhay byay thyay aystay
Otay earhay uetray iftshray. Omecay, adammay, et’slay awayay,

exEunt[_ay Ontaguemay anday Adylay Ontague._may]

ENVOLIObay.
Oodgay orrowmay, ousincay.

OMEOray.
Isay ethay ayday osay oungyay?

ENVOLIObay.
Utbay ewnay uckstray inenay.

OMEOray.
Ayay emay, adsay ourshay eemsay onglay.
Asway atthay myay atherfay atthay entway encehay osay astfay?

ENVOLIObay.
Itay asway. Atwhay adnesssay engthenslay Omeo’sray ourshay?

OMEOray.
Otnay avinghay atthay ichwhay, avinghay, akesmay emthay ortshay.

ENVOLIObay.
Inay ovelay?

OMEOray.
Outay.

ENVOLIObay.
Ofay ovelay?

OMEOray.
Outay ofay erhay avourfay erewhay Iay amay inay ovelay.

ENVOLIObay.
Alasay atthay ovelay osay entlegay inay ishay iewvay,
Ouldshay ebay osay annoustyray anday oughray inay oofpray.

OMEOray.
Alasay atthay ovelay, osewhay iewvay isay uffledmay illstay,
Ouldshay, ithoutway eyesay, eesay athwayspay otay ishay illway!
Erewhay allshay eway ineday? Oay emay! Atwhay ayfray asway erehay?
Etyay elltay emay otnay, orfay Iay avehay eardhay itay allay.
Ere’shay uchmay otay oday ithway atehay, utbay oremay ithway ovelay:
Whyay, enthay, Oay awlingbray ovelay! Oay ovinglay atehay!
Oay anythingay, ofay othingnay irstfay eatecray!
Oay eavyhay ightnesslay! erioussay anityvay!
Isshapenmay aoschay ofay ell-seemingway ormsfay!
Eatherfay ofay eadlay, ightbray okesmay, oldcay irefay, icksay ealthhay!
Ill-wakingstay eepslay, atthay isay otnay atwhay itay isay!
Isthay ovelay eelfay Iay, atthay eelfay onay ovelay inay isthay.
Ostday outhay otnay aughlay?

ENVOLIObay.
Onay ozcay, Iay atherray eepway.

OMEOray.
Oodgay earthay, atay atwhay?

ENVOLIObay.
Atay thyay oodgay eart’shay oppressionay.

OMEOray.
Whyay uchsay isay ove’slay ansgressiontray.
Iefsgray ofay inemay ownay ielay eavyhay inay myay eastbray,
Ichwhay outhay iltway opagatepray otay avehay itay estpray
Ithway oremay ofay inethay. Isthay ovelay atthay outhay asthay ownshay
Othday adday oremay iefgray otay ootay uchmay ofay inemay ownay.
Ovelay isay aay okesmay ademay ithway ethay umefay ofay ighssay;
Eingbay urg’dpay, aay irefay arklingspay inay overslay’ eyesay;
Eingbay ex’dvay, aay easay ourish’dnay ithway overslay’ earstay:
Atwhay isay itay elseay? Aay adnessmay ostmay iscreetday,
Aay okingchay allgay, anday aay eservingpray eetsway.
Arewellfay, myay ozcay.

oiNg._[_gay]

ENVOLIObay.
Oftsay! Iay illway ogay alongay:
Anday ifay ouyay eavelay emay osay, ouyay oday emay ongwray.

OMEOray.
Uttay! Iay avehay ostlay elfmysay; Iay amay otnay erehay.
Isthay isay otnay Omeoray, e’shay omesay otheray erewhay.

ENVOLIObay.
Elltay emay inay adnesssay owhay isay atthay ouyay ovelay?

OMEOray.
Atwhay, allshay Iay oangray anday elltay eethay?

ENVOLIObay.
Oangray! Whyay, onay; utbay adlysay elltay emay owhay.

OMEOray.
Idbay aay icksay anmay inay adnesssay akemay ishay illway,
Aay ordway illay urg’day otay oneay atthay isay osay illay.
Inay adnesssay, ousincay, Iay oday ovelay aay omanway.

ENVOLIObay.
Iay aim’day osay earnay enwhay Iay uppos’dsay ouyay ov’dlay.

OMEOray.
Aay ightray oodgay arkmanmay, anday e’sshay airfay Iay ovelay.

ENVOLIObay.
Aay ightray airfay arkmay, airfay ozcay, isay oonestsay ithay.

OMEOray.
Ellway, inay atthay ithay ouyay issmay: e’llshay otnay ebay ithay
Ithway Upid’scay arroway, eshay athhay Ian’sday itway;
Anday inay ongstray oofpray ofay astitychay ellway arm’day,
Omfray ove’slay eakway ildishchay owbay eshay iveslay uncharm’day.
Eshay illway otnay aystay ethay iegesay ofay ovinglay ermstay
Ornay idebay encounterth’ay ofay assailingay eyesay,
Ornay opeay erhay aplay otay aint-seducingsay oldgay:
Oay e’sshay ichray inay eautybay, onlyay oorpay
Atthay enwhay eshay iesday, ithway eautybay iesday erhay orestay.

ENVOLIObay.
Enthay eshay athhay ornsway atthay eshay illway illstay ivelay astechay?

OMEOray.
Eshay athhay, anday inay atthay aringspay akesmay ugehay asteway;
Orfay eautybay arv’dstay ithway erhay everitysay,
Utscay eautybay offay omfray allay osteritypay.
Eshay isay ootay airfay, ootay iseway; iselyway ootay airfay,
Otay eritmay issblay byay akingmay emay espairday.
Eshay athhay orswornfay otay ovelay, anday inay atthay owvay
Oday Iay ivelay eadday, atthay ivelay otay elltay itay ownay.

ENVOLIObay.
Ebay ul’dray byay emay, orgetfay otay inkthay ofay erhay.

OMEOray.
Oay eachtay emay owhay Iay ouldshay orgetfay otay inkthay.

ENVOLIObay.
Byay ivinggay ibertylay untoay inethay eyesay;
Examineay otheray eautiesbay.

OMEOray.
iS’tay ethay ayway
Otay allcay ershay, exquisiteay, inay uestionqay oremay.
Esethay appyhay asksmay atthay isskay airfay adieslay’ owsbray,
Eingbay ackblay, utspay usay inay indmay eythay idehay ethay airfay;
Ehay atthay isay uckenstray indblay annotcay orgetfay
Ethay eciouspray easuretray ofay ishay eyesightay ostlay.
Owshay emay aay istressmay atthay isay assingpay airfay,
Atwhay othday erhay eautybay ervesay utbay asay aay otenay
Erewhay Iay aymay eadray owhay ass’dpay atthay assingpay airfay?
Arewellfay, outhay anstcay otnay eachtay emay otay orgetfay.

ENVOLIObay.
I’llay aypay atthay octrineday, oray elseay ieday inay ebtday.

exEunt._[_ay]

ENEScay Iiay. Aay Eetstray.

Enteray Apuletcay, Arispay anday Ervantsay.

APULETcay.
Utbay Ontaguemay isay oundbay asay ellway asay Iay,
Inay enaltypay alikeay; anday is’tay otnay ardhay, Iay inkthay,
Orfay enmay osay olday asay eway otay eepkay ethay eacepay.

ARISpay.
Ofay onourablehay eckoningray areay ouyay othbay,
Anday itypay is’tay ouyay iv’dlay atay oddsay osay onglay.
Utbay ownay myay ordlay, atwhay aysay ouyay otay myay uitsay?

APULETcay.
Utbay ayingsay o’eray atwhay Iay avehay aidsay eforebay.
Myay ildchay isay etyay aay angerstray inay ethay orldway,
Eshay athhay otnay eensay ethay angechay ofay ourteenfay earsyay;
Etlay otway oremay ummerssay itherway inay eirthay idepray
Ereay eway aymay inkthay erhay iperay otay ebay aay idebray.

ARISpay.
Oungeryay anthay eshay areay appyhay othersmay ademay.

APULETcay.
Anday ootay oonsay arr’dmay areay osethay osay earlyay ademay.
Ethay earthay athhay allowedsway allay myay opeshay utbay eshay,
Eshay isay ethay opefulhay adylay ofay myay earthay:
Utbay ooway erhay, entlegay Arispay, etgay erhay earthay,
Myay illway otay erhay onsentcay isay utbay aay artpay;
Anday eshay agreeay, ithinway erhay opescay ofay oicechay
Ieslay myay onsentcay anday airfay accordingay oicevay.
Isthay ightnay Iay oldhay anay olday accustom’day eastfay,
Eretowhay Iay avehay inviteday anymay aay uestgay,
Uchsay asay Iay ovelay, anday ouyay amongay ethay orestay,
Oneay oremay, ostmay elcomeway, akesmay myay umbernay oremay.
Atay myay oorpay ousehay ooklay otay eholdbay isthay ightnay
Earth-treadingay arsstay atthay akemay arkday eavenhay ightlay:
Uchsay omfortcay asay oday ustylay oungyay enmay eelfay
Enwhay ellway apparell’day Aprilay onay ethay eelhay
Ofay impinglay interway eadstray, evenay uchsay elightday
Amongay eshfray emalefay udsbay allshay ouyay isthay ightnay
Inheritay atay myay ousehay. Earhay allay, allay eesay,
Anday ikelay erhay ostmay osewhay eritmay ostmay allshay ebay:
Ichwhay, onay oremay iewvay ofay anymay, inemay, eingbay oneay,
Aymay andstay inay umbernay, oughthay inay eckoningray onenay.
Omecay, ogay ithway emay. Ogay, irrahsay, udgetray aboutay
Oughthray airfay Eronavay; indfay osethay ersonspay outay
Osewhay amesnay areay ittenwray erethay, ives[_gay aay aper_pay] anday otay emthay aysay,
Myay ousehay anday elcomeway onay eirthay easureplay aystay.

exEunt[_ay Apuletcay anday Aris._pay]

ERVANTsay.
Indfay emthay outay osewhay amesnay areay ittenwray erehay! Itay isay ittenwray atthay ethay
oemakershay ouldshay eddlemay ithway ishay ardyay anday ethay ailortay ithway ishay astlay, ethay
isherfay ithway ishay encilpay, anday ethay ainterpay ithway ishay etsnay; utbay Iay amay entsay otay
indfay osethay ersonspay osewhay amesnay areay erehay itwray, anday ancay evernay indfay atwhay
amesnay ethay itingwray ersonpay athhay erehay itwray. Iay ustmay otay ethay earnedlay. Inay oodgay
imetay!

Enteray Envoliobay anday Omeoray.

ENVOLIObay.
Uttay, anmay, oneay irefay urnsbay outay another’say urningbay,
Oneay ainpay isay essen’dlay byay another’say anguishay;
Urntay iddygay, anday ebay olphay byay ackwardbay urningtay;
Oneay esperateday iefgray urescay ithway another’say anguishlay:
Aketay outhay omesay ewnay infectionay otay thyay eyeay,
Anday ethay ankray oisonpay ofay ethay olday illway ieday.

OMEOray.
Ouryay antainplay eaflay isay excellentay orfay atthay.

ENVOLIObay.
Orfay atwhay, Iay aypray eethay?

OMEOray.
Orfay ouryay okenbray inshay.

ENVOLIObay.
Whyay, Omeoray, artay outhay admay?

OMEOray.
Otnay admay, utbay oundbay oremay anthay aay admanmay isay:
Utshay upay inay isonpray, eptkay ithoutway myay oodfay,
Ipp’dwhay anday ormentedtay and—God-denay, oodgay ellowfay.

ERVANTsay.
Odgay igay’ o-dengay. Iay aypray, irsay, ancay ouyay eadray?

OMEOray.
Ayay, inemay ownay ortunefay inay myay iserymay.

ERVANTsay.
Erhapspay ouyay avehay earnedlay itay ithoutway ookbay.
Utbay Iay aypray, ancay ouyay eadray anythingay ouyay eesay?

OMEOray.
Ayay, Ifay Iay owknay ethay etterslay anday ethay anguagelay.

ERVANTsay.
Eyay aysay onestlyhay, estray ouyay errymay!

OMEOray.
Aystay, ellowfay; Iay ancay eadray.

e[_hay eadsray ethay etter._lay]

iGnior_say Artinomay anday ishay ifeway anday aughtersday;
Ountycay Anselmoay anday ishay eauteousbay isterssay;
Ethay adylay idowway ofay Utruvioay;
Igniorsay Acentioplay anday ishay ovelylay iecesnay;
Ercutiomay anday ishay otherbray Alentinevay;
Inemay uncleay Apuletcay, ishay ifeway, anday aughtersday;
Myay airfay iecenay Osalineray anday Ivialay;
Igniorsay Alentiovay anday ishay ousincay Alttybay;
Uciolay anday ethay ivelylay Elenahay. _


Aay airfay assemblyay. ivEs[_gay ackbay ethay aper_pay] Itherwhay ouldshay eythay omecay?

ERVANTsay.
Upay.

OMEOray.
Itherwhay otay uppersay?

ERVANTsay.
Otay ouray ousehay.

OMEOray.
Osewhay ousehay?

ERVANTsay.
Myay aster’smay.

OMEOray.
Indeeday Iay ouldshay avehay ask’day ouyay atthay eforebay.

ERVANTsay.
Ownay I’llay elltay ouyay ithoutway askingay. Myay astermay isay ethay eatgray ichray Apuletcay,
anday ifay ouyay ebay otnay ofay ethay ousehay ofay Ontaguesmay, Iay aypray omecay anday ushcray aay
upcay ofay ineway. Estray ouyay errymay.

exIt._[_ay]

ENVOLIObay.
Atay isthay amesay ancientay eastfay ofay Apulet’scay
Upssay ethay airfay Osalineray omwhay outhay osay ov’stlay;
Ithway allay ethay admireday eautiesbay ofay Eronavay.
Ogay itherthay anday ithway unattainteday eyeay,
Omparecay erhay acefay ithway omesay atthay Iay allshay owshay,
Anday Iay illway akemay eethay inkthay thyay answay aay owcray.

OMEOray.
Enwhay ethay evoutday eligionray ofay inemay eyeay
Aintainsmay uchsay alsehoodfay, enthay urntay earstay otay irefay;
Anday esethay owhay, oftenay own’ddray, ouldcay evernay ieday,
Ansparenttray ereticshay, ebay urntbay orfay iarslay.
Oneay airerfay anthay myay ovelay? Ethay all-seeingay unsay
E’ernay awsay erhay atchmay incesay irstfay ethay orldway egunbay.

ENVOLIObay.
Uttay, ouyay awsay erhay airfay, onenay elseay eingbay byay,
Erselfhay ois’dpay ithway erselfhay inay eitheray eyeay:
Utbay inay atthay alcrystay alesscay etlay erethay ebay eigh’dway
Ouryay ady’slay ovelay againstay omesay otheray aidmay
Atthay Iay illway owshay ouyay iningshay atay isthay eastfay,
Anday eshay allshay antscay owshay ellway atthay ownay owsshay estbay.

OMEOray.
I’llay ogay alongay, onay uchsay ightsay otay ebay ownshay,
Utbay otay ejoiceray inay endoursplay ofay myay ownay.

exEunt._[_ay]

ENEScay IIiay. Oomray inay Apulet’scay Ousehay.

Enteray Adylay Apuletcay anday Ursenay.

ADYlay APULETcay.
Ursenay, ere’swhay myay aughterday? Allcay erhay orthfay otay emay.

URSEnay.
Ownay, byay myay aidenheadmay, atay elvetway earyay olday,
Iay adebay erhay omecay. Atwhay, amblay! Atwhay adybirdlay!
Odgay orbidfay! Ere’swhay isthay irlgay? Atwhay, Ulietjay!

Enteray Ulietjay.

ULIETjay.
Owhay ownay, owhay allscay?

URSEnay.
Ouryay othermay.

ULIETjay.
Adammay, Iay amay erehay. Atwhay isay ouryay illway?

ADYlay APULETcay.
Isthay isay ethay attermay. Ursenay, ivegay eavelay awhileay,
Eway ustmay alktay inay ecretsay. Ursenay, omecay ackbay againay,
Iay avehay emember’dray emay, ou’sthay earhay ouray ounselcay.
Outhay owestknay myay aughter’sday ofay aay ettypray ageay.

URSEnay.
Aithfay, Iay ancay elltay erhay ageay untoay anay ourhay.

ADYlay APULETcay.
E’sshay otnay ourteenfay.

URSEnay.
I’llay aylay ourteenfay ofay myay eethtay,
Anday etyay, otay myay eentay ebay itay okenspay, Iay avehay utbay ourfay,
Eshay isay otnay ourteenfay. Owhay onglay isay itay ownay
Otay Ammas-tidelay?

ADYlay APULETcay.
Aay ortnightfay anday odday aysday.

URSEnay.
Evenay oray odday, ofay allay aysday inay ethay earyay,
Omecay Ammaslay Eveay atay ightnay allshay eshay ebay ourteenfay.
Usansay anday e,—goDshay estray allay Istianchray ouls!say—
Ereway ofay anay ageay. Ellway, Usansay isay ithway Odgay;
Eshay asway ootay oodgay orfay emay. Utbay asay Iay aidsay,
Onay Ammaslay Eveay atay ightnay allshay eshay ebay ourteenfay;
Atthay allshay eshay, arrymay; Iay ememberray itay ellway.
iS’tay incesay ethay earthquakeay ownay elevenay earsyay;
Anday eshay asway ean’d,—iway evernay allshay orgetfay it—ay,
Ofay allay ethay aysday ofay ethay earyay, uponay atthay ayday:
Orfay Iay adhay enthay aidlay ormwoodway otay myay ugday,
Ittingsay inay ethay unsay underay ethay ovehouseday allway;
Myay ordlay anday ouyay ereway enthay atay Antuamay:
Aynay, Iay oday earbay aay ainbray. Utbay asay Iay aidsay,
Enwhay itay idday astetay ethay ormwoodway onay ethay ipplenay
Ofay myay ugday anday eltfay itay itterbay, ettypray oolfay,
Otay eesay itay etchytay, anday allfay outay ithway ethay ugday!
Akeshay, uothqay ethay ovehouseday: as’tway onay eednay, Iay owtray,
Otay idbay emay udgetray.
Anday incesay atthay imetay itay isay elevenay earsyay;
Orfay enthay eshay ouldcay andstay aloneay; aynay, byay oodth’ray
Eshay ouldcay avehay unray anday addledway allay aboutay;
Orfay evenay ethay ayday eforebay eshay okebray erhay owbray,
Anday enthay myay usband,—gOdhay ebay ithway ishay oulsay!
Aay asway aay errymay an,—tookmay upay ethay ildchay:
eA,‘yay’ uothqay ehay, ost‘day outhay allfay uponay thyay acefay?
Outhay iltway allfay ackwardbay enwhay outhay asthay oremay itway;
Iltway outhay otnay, Ule?jay’ anday, byay myay olidamehay,
Ethay ettypray etchwray eftlay ingcryay, anday aidsay aY’‘ay.
Otay eesay ownay owhay aay estjay allshay omecay aboutay.
Iay arrantway, anday Iay ouldshay ivelay aay ousandthay earsyay,
Iay evernay ouldshay orgetfay itay. iLt‘way outhay otnay, Ule?jay’ uothqay ehay;
Anday, ettypray oolfay, itay intedstay, anday aidsay aY.‘ay’

ADYlay APULETcay.
Enoughay ofay isthay; Iay aypray eethay oldhay thyay eacepay.

URSEnay.
Esyay, adammay, etyay Iay annotcay oosechay utbay aughlay,
Otay inkthay itay ouldshay eavelay ingcryay, anday aysay aY’‘ay;
Anday etyay Iay arrantway itay adhay uponay itay owbray
Aay umpbay asay igbay asay aay oungyay ockerel’scay onestay;
Aay erilouspay ockknay, anday itay iedcray itterlybay.
eA,‘yay’ uothqay myay usbandhay, all’st‘fay uponay thyay acefay?
Outhay iltway allfay ackwardbay enwhay outhay omestcay otay ageay;
Iltway outhay otnay, Ule?jay’ itay intedstay, anday aidsay aY’‘ay.

ULIETjay.
Anday intstay outhay ootay, Iay aypray eethay, Ursenay, aysay Iay.

URSEnay.
Eacepay, Iay avehay oneday. Odgay arkmay eethay otay ishay acegray
Outhay astway ethay ettiestpray abebay atthay e’eray Iay urs’dnay:
Anday Iay ightmay ivelay otay eesay eethay arriedmay onceay, Iay avehay myay ishway.

ADYlay APULETcay.
Arrymay, atthay arrymay isay ethay eryvay emethay
Iay amecay otay alktay ofay. Elltay emay, aughterday Ulietjay,
Owhay andsstay ouryay ispositionday otay ebay arriedmay?

ULIETjay.
Itay isay anay onourhay atthay Iay eamdray otnay ofay.

URSEnay.
Anay onourhay! Ereway otnay Iay inethay onlyay ursenay,
Iay ouldway aysay outhay adsthay uck’dsay isdomway omfray thyay eattay.

ADYlay APULETcay.
Ellway, inkthay ofay arriagemay ownay: oungeryay anthay ouyay,
Erehay inay Eronavay, adieslay ofay esteemay,
Areay ademay alreadyay othersmay. Byay myay ountcay
Iay asway ouryay othermay uchmay uponay esethay earsyay
Atthay ouyay areay ownay aay aidmay. Usthay, enthay, inay iefbray;
Ethay aliantvay Arispay eekssay ouyay orfay ishay ovelay.

URSEnay.
Aay anmay, oungyay adylay! Adylay, uchsay aay anmay
Asay allay ethay orld—whyway e’shay aay anmay ofay axway.

ADYlay APULETcay.
Erona’svay ummersay athhay otnay uchsay aay owerflay.

URSEnay.
Aynay, e’shay aay owerflay, inay aithfay aay eryvay owerflay.

ADYlay APULETcay.
Atwhay aysay ouyay, ancay ouyay ovelay ethay entlemangay?
Isthay ightnay ouyay allshay eholdbay imhay atay ouray eastfay;
Eadray o’eray ethay olumevay ofay oungyay Arispay’ acefay,
Anday indfay elightday itwray erethay ithway eauty’sbay enpay.
Examineay everyay arriedmay ineamentlay,
Anday eesay owhay oneay anotheray endslay ontentcay;
Anday atwhay obscur’day inay isthay airfay olumevay ieslay,
Indfay ittenwray inay ethay argentmay ofay ishay eyesay.
Isthay eciouspray ookbay ofay ovelay, isthay unbounday overlay,
Otay eautifybay imhay, onlyay ackslay aay overcay:
Ethay ishfay iveslay inay ethay easay; anday is’tay uchmay idepray
Orfay airfay ithoutway ethay airfay ithinway otay idehay.
Atthay ookbay inay any’smay eyesay othday areshay ethay oryglay,
Atthay inay oldgay aspsclay ockslay inay ethay oldengay orystay;
Osay allshay ouyay areshay allay atthay ehay othday ossesspay,
Byay avinghay imhay, akingmay ourselfyay onay esslay.

URSEnay.
Onay esslay, aynay iggerbay. Omenway owgray byay enmay.

ADYlay APULETcay.
Eakspay ieflybray, ancay ouyay ikelay ofay Arispay’ ovelay?

ULIETjay.
I’llay ooklay otay ikelay, ifay ookinglay ikinglay ovemay:
Utbay onay oremay eepday illway Iay endartay inemay eyeay
Anthay ouryay onsentcay ivesgay engthstray otay akemay itay flyay.

Enteray aay Ervantsay.

ERVANTsay.
Adammay, ethay uestsgay areay omecay, uppersay ervedsay upay, ouyay alledcay, myay oungyay adylay
askeday orfay, ethay Ursenay ursedcay inay ethay antrypay, anday everythingay inay extremityay.
Iay ustmay encehay otay aitway, Iay eseechbay ouyay ollowfay aightstray.

ADYlay APULETcay.
Eway ollowfay eethay.

exIt[_ay Ervant._say]

Ulietjay, ethay Ountycay aysstay.

URSEnay.
Ogay, irlgay, eeksay appyhay ightsnay otay appyhay aysday.

exEunt._[_ay]

ENEScay Ivay. Aay Eetstray.

Enteray Omeoray, Ercutiomay, Envoliobay, ithway ivefay oray ixsay Askersmay;
Orch-bearerstay anday othersay.

OMEOray.
Atwhay, allshay isthay eechspay ebay okespay orfay ouray excuseay?
Oray allshay eway onay ithoutway apologyay?

ENVOLIObay.
Ethay ateday isay outay ofay uchsay olixitypray:
E’llway avehay onay Upidcay oodwink’dhay ithway aay arfscay,
Earingbay aay Artar’stay aintedpay owbay ofay athlay,
Aringscay ethay adieslay ikelay aay ow-keepercray;
Ornay onay ithout-bookway ologuepray, aintlyfay okespay
Afteray ethay ompterpray, orfay ouray entranceay:
Utbay etlay emthay easuremay usay byay atwhay eythay illway,
E’llway easuremay emthay aay easuremay, anday ebay onegay.

OMEOray.
Ivegay emay aay orchtay, Iay amay otnay orfay isthay amblingay;
Eingbay utbay eavyhay Iay illway earbay ethay ightlay.

ERCUTIOmay.
Aynay, entlegay Omeoray, eway ustmay avehay ouyay anceday.

OMEOray.
Otnay Iay, elievebay emay, ouyay avehay ancingday oesshay,
Ithway imblenay olessay, Iay avehay aay oulsay ofay eadlay
Osay akesstay emay otay ethay oundgray Iay annotcay ovemay.

ERCUTIOmay.
Ouyay areay aay overlay, orrowbay Upid’scay ingsway,
Anday oarsay ithway emthay aboveay aay ommoncay oundbay.

OMEOray.
Iay amay ootay oresay enpierceday ithway ishay aftshay
Otay oarsay ithway ishay ightlay eathersfay, anday osay oundbay,
Iay annotcay oundbay aay itchpay aboveay ullday oeway.
Underay ove’slay eavyhay urdenbay oday Iay inksay.

ERCUTIOmay.
Anday, otay inksay inay itay, ouldshay ouyay urdenbay ovelay;
Ootay eatgray oppressionay orfay aay endertay ingthay.

OMEOray.
Isay ovelay aay endertay ingthay? Itay isay ootay oughray,
Ootay uderay, ootay oisterousbay; anday itay ickspray ikelay ornthay.

ERCUTIOmay.
Ifay ovelay ebay oughray ithway ouyay, ebay oughray ithway ovelay;
Ickpray ovelay orfay ickingpray, anday ouyay eatbay ovelay ownday.
Ivegay emay aay asecay otay utpay myay isagevay inay: utTing[_pay onay aay ask._may]
Aay isorvay orfay aay isorvay. Atwhay arecay Iay
Atwhay uriouscay eyeay othday uoteqay eformitiesday?
Erehay areay ethay eetle-browsbay allshay ushblay orfay emay.

ENVOLIObay.
Omecay, ockknay anday enteray; anday onay oonersay inay
Utbay everyay anmay etakebay imhay otay ishay egslay.

OMEOray.
Aay orchtay orfay emay: etlay antonsway, ightlay ofay earthay,
Ickletay ethay enselesssay ushesray ithway eirthay eelshay;
Orfay Iay amay overb’dpray ithway aay andsiregray asephray,
I’llay ebay aay andle-holdercay anday ooklay onay,
Ethay amegay asway e’ernay osay airfay, anday Iay amay oneday.

ERCUTIOmay.
Uttay, un’sday ethay ousemay, ethay onstable’scay ownay ordway:
Ifay outhay artay unday, e’llway awdray eethay omfray ethay iremay
Oray avesay ouryay everenceray ovelay, ereinwhay outhay ickeststay
Upay otay ethay earsay. Omecay, eway urnbay aylightday, ohay.

OMEOray.
Aynay, at’sthay otnay osay.

ERCUTIOmay.
Iay eanmay irsay, inay elayday
Eway asteway ouray ightslay inay ainvay, ightlay ightslay byay ayday.
Aketay ouray oodgay eaningmay, orfay ouray udgmentjay itssay
Ivefay imestay inay atthay ereay onceay inay ouray ivefay itsway.

OMEOray.
Anday eway eanmay ellway inay oinggay otay isthay askmay;
Utbay is’tay onay itway otay ogay.

ERCUTIOmay.
Whyay, aymay oneay askay?

OMEOray.
Iay eamtdray aay eamdray onighttay.

ERCUTIOmay.
Anday osay idday Iay.

OMEOray.
Ellway atwhay asway oursyay?

ERCUTIOmay.
Atthay eamersdray oftenay ielay.

OMEOray.
Inay edbay asleepay, ilewhay eythay oday eamdray ingsthay uetray.

ERCUTIOmay.
Oay, enthay, Iay eesay Ueenqay Abmay athhay eenbay ithway ouyay.
Eshay isay ethay airiesfay’ idwifemay, anday eshay omescay
Inay apeshay onay iggerbay anthay anay agate-stoneay
Onay ethay ore-fingerfay ofay anay aldermanay,
Awndray ithway aay eamtay ofay ittlelay atomiesay
Overay en’smay osesnay asay eythay ielay asleepay:
Erhay aggon-spokesway ademay ofay onglay innersspay’ egslay;
Ethay overcay, ofay ethay ingsway ofay asshoppersgray;
Erhay acestray, ofay ethay allestsmay ider’sspay ebway;
Ethay ollarscay, ofay ethay oonshine’smay ateryway eamsbay;
Erhay ipwhay ofay icket’scray onebay; ethay ashlay, ofay ilmfay;
Erhay aggonerway, aay allsmay ey-coatedgray atgnay,
Otnay alfhay osay igbay asay aay oundray ittlelay ormway
Ick’dpray omfray ethay azylay ingerfay ofay aay aidmay:
Erhay ariotchay isay anay emptyay azelnuthay,
Ademay byay ethay oinerjay uirrelsqay oray olday ubgray,
Imetay outay oay’ indmay ethay airiesfay’ oachmakerscay.
Anday inay isthay atestay eshay allopsgay ightnay byay ightnay
Oughthray overslay’ ainsbray, anday enthay eythay eamdray ofay ovelay;
O’eray ourtierscay’ eesknay, atthay eamdray onay urtsiescay aightstray;
O’eray awyerslay’ ingersfay, owhay aightstray eamdray onay eesfay;
O’eray adieslay’ ipslay, owhay aightstray onay isseskay eamdray,
Ichwhay oftay ethay angryay Abmay ithway istersblay aguesplay,
Ecausebay eirthay eathsbray ithway eetmeatssway aintedtay areay:
Ometimesay eshay allopsgay o’eray aay ourtier’scay osenay,
Anday enthay eamsdray ehay ofay ellingsmay outay aay uitsay;
Anday ometimesay omescay eshay ithway aay ithe-pig’stay ailtay,
Icklingtay aay arson’spay osenay asay aay ieslay asleepay,
Enthay eamsdray ehay ofay anotheray eneficebay:
Ometimesay eshay ivethdray o’eray aay oldier’ssay ecknay,
Anday enthay eamsdray ehay ofay uttingcay oreignfay oatsthray,
Ofay eachesbray, ambuscadosay, Anishspay adesblay,
Ofay ealthshay ivefay athomfay eepday; anday enthay anonay
Umsdray inay ishay earay, atay ichwhay ehay artsstay anday akesway;
Anday, eingbay usthay ightedfray, earssway aay ayerpray oray otway,
Anday eepsslay againay. Isthay isay atthay eryvay Abmay
Atthay atsplay ethay anesmay ofay orseshay inay ethay ightnay;
Anday akesbay ethay elf-locksay inay oulfay uttishslay airshay,
Ichwhay, onceay untangleday, uchmay isfortunemay odesbay:
Isthay isay ethay aghay, enwhay aidsmay ielay onay eirthay acksbay,
Atthay essespray emthay, anday earnslay emthay irstfay otay earbay,
Akingmay emthay omenway ofay oodgay arriagecay:
Isthay isay e,shay—

OMEOray.
Eacepay, eacepay, Ercutiomay, eacepay,
Outhay alk’sttay ofay othingnay.

ERCUTIOmay.
Uetray, Iay alktay ofay eamsdray,
Ichwhay areay ethay ildrenchay ofay anay idleay ainbray,
Egotbay ofay othingnay utbay ainvay antasyfay,
Ichwhay isay asay inthay ofay ubstancesay asay ethay airay,
Anday oremay inconstantay anthay ethay indway, owhay oosway
Evenay ownay ethay ozenfray osombay ofay ethay orthnay,
Anday, eingbay anger’day, uffspay awayay omfray encethay,
Urningtay ishay idesay otay ethay ew-droppingday outhsay.

ENVOLIObay.
Isthay indway ouyay alktay ofay owsblay usay omfray ourselvesay:
Uppersay isay oneday, anday eway allshay omecay ootay atelay.

OMEOray.
Iay earfay ootay earlyay: orfay myay indmay isgivesmay
Omesay onsequencecay etyay anginghay inay ethay arsstay,
Allshay itterlybay eginbay ishay earfulfay ateday
Ithway isthay ight’snay evelsray; anday expireay ethay ermtay
Ofay aay espisedday ifelay, os’dclay inay myay eastbray
Byay omesay ilevay orfeitfay ofay untimelyay eathday.
Utbay ehay atthay athhay ethay eeragestay ofay myay oursecay
Irectday myay uitsay. Onay, ustylay entlemengay!

ENVOLIObay.
Ikestray, umdray.

exEunt._[_ay]

ENEScay Vay. Aay Allhay inay Apulet’scay Ousehay.

Usiciansmay aitingway. Enteray Ervantssay.

IRSTfay ERVANTsay.
Ere’swhay Otpanpay, atthay ehay elpshay otnay otay aketay awayay?
Ehay iftshay aay enchertray! Ehay apescray aay enchertray!

ECONDsay ERVANTsay.
Enwhay oodgay annersmay allshay ielay allay inay oneay oray otway en’smay andshay, anday eythay
unwash’day ootay, is’tay aay oulfay ingthay.

IRSTfay ERVANTsay.
Awayay ithway ethay oin-stoolsjay, emoveray ethay ourt-cupboardcay, ooklay otay ethay
ateplay. Oodgay outhay, avesay emay aay iecepay ofay archpanemay; anday asay outhay oveslay emay,
etlay ethay orterpay etlay inay Usansay Indstonegray anday Ellnay. Antonyay anday Otpanpay!

ECONDsay ERVANTsay.
Ayay, oybay, eadyray.

IRSTfay ERVANTsay.
Ouyay areay ookedlay orfay anday alledcay orfay, askeday orfay anday oughtsay orfay, inay ethay
eatgray amberchay.

ECONDsay ERVANTsay.
Eway annotcay ebay erehay anday erethay ootay. Eerlychay, oysbay. Ebay iskbray awhileay, anday
ethay ongerlay iverlay aketay allay.

exEunt._[_ay]

Enteray Apuletcay, &cay. ithway ethay Uestsgay anday Entlewomengay otay ethay Askersmay.

APULETcay.
Elcomeway, entlemengay, adieslay atthay avehay eirthay oestay
Unplagu’day ithway ornscay illway avehay aay outbay ithway ouyay.
Ahay myay istressesmay, ichwhay ofay ouyay allay
Illway ownay enyday otay anceday? Eshay atthay akesmay aintyday,
Eshay I’llay earsway athhay ornscay. Amay Iay omecay earnay eyay ownay?
Elcomeway, entlemengay! Iay avehay eensay ethay ayday
Atthay Iay avehay ornway aay isorvay, anday ouldcay elltay
Aay isperingwhay aletay inay aay airfay ady’slay earay,
Uchsay asay ouldway easeplay; is’tay onegay, is’tay onegay, is’tay onegay,
Ouyay areay elcomeway, entlemengay! Omecay, usiciansmay, ayplay.
Aay allhay, aay allhay, ivegay oomray! Anday ootfay itay, irlsgay.

usIc[_may aysplay, anday eythay ance._day]

Oremay ightlay, ouyay avesknay; anday urntay ethay ablestay upay,
Anday uenchqay ethay irefay, ethay oomray isay owngray ootay othay.
Ahay irrahsay, isthay unlook’d-foray ortspay omescay ellway.
Aynay itsay, aynay itsay, oodgay ousincay Apuletcay,
Orfay ouyay anday Iay areay astpay ouray ancingday aysday;
Owhay onglay is’tay ownay incesay astlay ourselfyay anday Iay
Ereway inay aay askmay?

APULET’scay OUSINcay.
By’ray Adylay, irtythay earsyay.

APULETcay.
Atwhay, anmay, is’tay otnay osay uchmay, is’tay otnay osay uchmay:
iS’tay incesay ethay uptialnay ofay Ucentiolay,
Omecay Entecostpay asay uicklyqay asay itay illway,
Omesay ivefay anday entytway earsyay; anday enthay eway ask’dmay.

APULET’scay OUSINcay.
iS’tay oremay, is’tay oremay, ishay onsay isay elderay, irsay;
Ishay onsay isay irtythay.

APULETcay.
Illway ouyay elltay emay atthay?
Ishay onsay asway utbay aay ardway otway earsyay agoay.

OMEOray.
Atwhay adylay isay atthay, ichwhay othday enrichay ethay andhay
Ofay onderyay ightknay?

ERVANTsay.
Iay owknay otnay, irsay.

OMEOray.
Oay, eshay othday eachtay ethay orchestay otay urnbay ightbray!
Itay eemssay eshay angshay uponay ethay eekchay ofay ightnay
Asay aay ichray eweljay inay anay Ethiop’say earay;
Eautybay ootay ichray orfay useay, orfay earthay ootay earday!
Osay owsshay aay owysnay oveday oopingtray ithway owscray
Asay onderyay adylay o’eray erhay ellowsfay owsshay.
Ethay easuremay oneday, I’llay atchway erhay aceplay ofay andstay,
Anday ouchingtay ershay, akemay essedblay myay uderay andhay.
Idday myay earthay ovelay illtay ownay? Orswearfay itay, ightsay!
Orfay Iay e’ernay awsay uetray eautybay illtay isthay ightnay.

ALTTYbay.
Isthay byay ishay oicevay, ouldshay ebay aay Ontaguemay.
Etchfay emay myay apierray, oybay. Atwhay, aresday ethay aveslay
Omecay itherhay, over’dcay ithway anay anticay acefay,
Otay eerflay anday ornscay atay ouray olemnitysay?
Ownay byay ethay ockstay anday onourhay ofay myay inkay,
Otay ikestray imhay eadday Iay oldhay itay otnay aay insay.

APULETcay.
Whyay owhay ownay, insmankay!
Ereforewhay ormstay ouyay osay?

ALTTYbay.
Uncleay, isthay isay aay Ontaguemay, ouray oefay;
Aay illainvay atthay isay itherhay omecay inay itespay,
Otay ornscay atay ouray olemnitysay isthay ightnay.

APULETcay.
Oungyay Omeoray, isay itay?

ALTTYbay.
iS’tay ehay, atthay illainvay Omeoray.

APULETcay.
Ontentcay eethay, entlegay ozcay, etlay imhay aloneay,
Aay earsbay imhay ikelay aay ortlypay entlemangay;
Anday, otay aysay uthtray, Eronavay agsbray ofay imhay
Otay ebay aay irtuousvay anday ell-govern’dway outhyay.
Iay ouldway otnay orfay ethay ealthway ofay allay ethay owntay
Erehay inay myay ousehay oday imhay isparagementday.
Ereforethay ebay atientpay, aketay onay otenay ofay imhay,
Itay isay myay illway; ethay ichwhay ifay outhay espectray,
Owshay aay airfay esencepray anday utpay offay esethay ownsfray,
Anay ill-beseemingay emblancesay orfay aay eastfay.

ALTTYbay.
Itay itsfay enwhay uchsay aay illainvay isay aay uestgay:
I’llay otnay endureay imhay.

APULETcay.
Ehay allshay ebay endur’day.
Atwhay, oodmangay oybay! Iay aysay ehay allshay, ogay otay;
Amay Iay ethay astermay erehay, oray ouyay? Ogay otay.
Ou’llyay otnay endureay imhay! Odgay allshay endmay myay oulsay,
Ou’llyay akemay aay utinymay amongay myay uestsgay!
Ouyay illway etsay ock-a-hoopcay, ou’llyay ebay ethay anmay!

ALTTYbay.
Whyay, uncleay, is’tay aay ameshay.

APULETcay.
Ogay otay, ogay otay!
Ouyay areay aay aucysay oybay. Is’tay osay, indeeday?
Isthay icktray aymay ancechay otay athescay ouyay, Iay owknay atwhay.
Ouyay ustmay ontrarycay emay! Arrymay, is’tay imetay.
Ellway aidsay, myay earts!—yOuhay areay aay incoxpray; ogay:
Ebay uietqay, or—Moreay ightlay, oremay ight!—fOrlay ameshay!
I’llay akemay ouyay uietqay. Atwhay, eerlychay, myay eartshay.

ALTTYbay.
Atiencepay erforcepay ithway ilfulway olerchay eetingmay
Akesmay myay eshflay embletray inay eirthay ifferentday eetinggray.
Iay illway ithdrawway: utbay isthay intrusionay allshay,
Ownay eemingsay eetsway, onvertcay otay itterbay allgay.

exIt._[_ay]

OMEOray.
o[_tay Uliet._jay] Ifay Iay ofanepray ithway myay unworthiestay andhay
Isthay olyhay ineshray, ethay entlegay insay isay isthay,
Myay ipslay, otway ushingblay ilgrimspay, eadyray andstay
Otay oothsmay atthay oughray ouchtay ithway aay endertay isskay.

ULIETjay.
Oodgay ilgrimpay, ouyay oday ongwray ouryay andhay ootay uchmay,
Ichwhay annerlymay evotionday owsshay inay isthay;
Orfay aintssay avehay andshay atthay ilgrimspay’ andshay oday ouchtay,
Anday almpay otay almpay isay olyhay almerspay’ isskay.

OMEOray.
Avehay otnay aintssay ipslay, anday olyhay almerspay ootay?

ULIETjay.
Ayay, ilgrimpay, ipslay atthay eythay ustmay useay inay ayerpray.

OMEOray.
Oay, enthay, earday aintsay, etlay ipslay oday atwhay andshay oday:
Eythay aypray, antgray outhay, estlay aithfay urntay otay espairday.

ULIETjay.
Aintssay oday otnay ovemay, oughthay antgray orfay ayerspray’ akesay.

OMEOray.
Enthay ovemay otnay ilewhay myay ayer’spray effectay Iay aketay.
Usthay omfray myay ipslay, byay inethay myay insay isay urg’dpay.
isSing[_kay er._hay]

ULIETjay.
Enthay avehay myay ipslay ethay insay atthay eythay avehay ooktay.

OMEOray.
Insay omfray myay ipslay? Oay espasstray eetlysway urg’day!
Ivegay emay myay insay againay.

ULIETjay.
Ouyay isskay byay ethay ookbay.

URSEnay.
Adammay, ouryay othermay avescray aay ordway ithway ouyay.

OMEOray.
Atwhay isay erhay othermay?

URSEnay.
Arrymay, achelorbay,
Erhay othermay isay ethay adylay ofay ethay ousehay,
Anday aay oodgay adylay, anday aay iseway anday irtuousvay.
Iay urs’dnay erhay aughterday atthay ouyay alk’dtay ithalway.
Iay elltay ouyay, ehay atthay ancay aylay oldhay ofay erhay
Allshay avehay ethay inkschay.

OMEOray.
Isay eshay aay Apuletcay?
Oay earday accountay! Myay ifelay isay myay oe’sfay ebtday.

ENVOLIObay.
Awayay, ebay onegay; ethay ortspay isay atay ethay estbay.

OMEOray.
Ayay, osay Iay earfay; ethay oremay isay myay unrestay.

APULETcay.
Aynay, entlemengay, eparepray otnay otay ebay onegay,
Eway avehay aay iflingtray oolishfay anquetbay owardstay.
Isay itay e’enay osay? Whyay enthay, Iay ankthay ouyay allay;
Iay ankthay ouyay, onesthay entlemengay; oodgay ightnay.
Oremay orchestay erehay! Omecay onay enthay, et’slay otay edbay.
Ahay, irrahsay, byay myay ayfay, itay axesway atelay,
I’llay otay myay estray.

exEunt[_ay allay utbay Ulietjay anday Urse._nay]

ULIETjay.
Omecay itherhay, Ursenay. Atwhay isay ondyay entlemangay?

URSEnay.
Ethay onsay anday eirhay ofay olday Iberiotay.

ULIETjay.
At’swhay ehay atthay ownay isay oinggay outay ofay oorday?

URSEnay.
Arrymay, atthay Iay inkthay ebay oungyay Etruchiopay.

ULIETjay.
At’swhay ehay atthay ollowsfay erehay, atthay ouldway otnay anceday?

URSEnay.
Iay owknay otnay.

ULIETjay.
Ogay askay ishay amenay. Ifay ehay ebay arriedmay,
Myay avegray isay ikelay otay ebay myay eddingway edbay.

URSEnay.
Ishay amenay isay Omeoray, anday aay Ontaguemay,
Ethay onlyay onsay ofay ouryay eatgray enemyay.

ULIETjay.
Myay onlyay ovelay ungspray omfray myay onlyay atehay!
Ootay earlyay eensay unknownay, anday ownknay ootay atelay!
Odigiouspray irthbay ofay ovelay itay isay otay emay,
Atthay Iay ustmay ovelay aay oathedlay enemyay.

URSEnay.
At’swhay isthay? At’swhay isthay?

ULIETjay.
Aay erhymay Iay earn’dlay evenay ownay
Ofay oneay Iay anc’dday ithalway.

onE[_ay allscay ithinway, uLiet’._‘jay]

URSEnay.
Anonay, anonay!
Omecay et’slay awayay, ethay angersstray allay areay onegay.

ACtay Iiay


Enteray Oruschay.

ORUSChay.
Ownay olday esireday othday inay ishay eathbedday ielay,
Anday oungyay affectionay apesgay otay ebay ishay eirhay;
Atthay airfay orfay ichwhay ovelay oan’dgray orfay anday ouldway ieday,
Ithway endertay Ulietjay atch’dmay, isay ownay otnay airfay.
Ownay Omeoray isay elov’dbay, anday oveslay againay,
Alikeay ewitchedbay byay ethay armchay ofay ookslay;
Utbay otay ishay oefay uppos’dsay ehay ustmay omplaincay,
Anday eshay ealstay ove’slay eetsway aitbay omfray earfulfay ookshay:
Eingbay eldhay aay oefay, ehay aymay otnay avehay accessay
Otay eathebray uchsay owsvay asay overslay useay otay earsway;
Anday eshay asay uchmay inay ovelay, erhay eansmay uchmay esslay
Otay eetmay erhay ewnay elovedbay anywhereay.
Utbay assionpay endslay emthay owerpay, imetay eansmay, otay eetmay,
Emperingtay extremitiesay ithway extremeay eetsway.

exIt._[_ay]

ENEScay Iay. Anay openay aceplay adjoiningay Apulet’scay Ardengay.

Enteray Omeoray.

OMEOray.
Ancay Iay ogay orwardfay enwhay myay earthay isay erehay?
Urntay ackbay, ullday earthay, anday indfay thyay entrecay outay.

e[_hay imbsclay ethay allway anday eapslay ownday ithinway it._ay]

Enteray Envoliobay anday Ercutiomay.

ENVOLIObay.
Omeoray! Myay ousincay Omeoray! Omeoray!

ERCUTIOmay.
Ehay isay iseway,
Anday onay myay ifelay athhay ol’nstay imhay omehay otay edbay.

ENVOLIObay.
Ehay anray isthay ayway, anday eap’dlay isthay orcharday allway:
Allcay, oodgay Ercutiomay.

ERCUTIOmay.
Aynay, I’llay onjurecay ootay.
Omeoray! Umourshay! Admanmay! Assionpay! Overlay!
Appearay outhay inay ethay ikenesslay ofay aay ighsay,
Eakspay utbay oneay erhymay, anday Iay amay atisfiedsay;
Cryay utbay aH‘ay e!may’ Onouncepray utbay Ovelay anday oveday;
Eakspay otay myay ossipgay Enusvay oneay airfay ordway,
Oneay icknamenay orfay erhay urblindpay onsay anday eirhay,
Oungyay Abrahamay Upidcay, ehay atthay otshay osay imtray
Enwhay Ingkay Ophetuacay ov’dlay ethay eggar-maidbay.
Ehay earethhay otnay, ehay irrethstay otnay, ehay ovethmay otnay;
Ethay apeay isay eadday, anday Iay ustmay onjurecay imhay.
Iay onjurecay eethay byay Osaline’sray ightbray eyesay,
Byay erhay ighhay oreheadfay anday erhay arletscay iplay,
Byay erhay inefay ootfay, aightstray eglay, anday uiveringqay ighthay,
Anday ethay emesnesday atthay erethay adjacentay ielay,
Atthay inay thyay ikenesslay outhay appearay otay usay.

ENVOLIObay.
Anay ifay ehay earhay eethay, outhay iltway angeray imhay.

ERCUTIOmay.
Isthay annotcay angeray imhay. oUld’tway angeray imhay
Otay aiseray aay iritspay inay ishay istressmay’ irclecay,
Ofay omesay angestray aturenay, ettinglay itay erethay andstay
Illtay eshay adhay aidlay itay, anday onjur’dcay itay ownday;
Atthay ereway omesay itespay. Myay invocationay
Isay airfay anday onesthay, anday, inay ishay istressmay’ amenay,
Iay onjurecay onlyay utbay otay aiseray upay imhay.

ENVOLIObay.
Omecay, ehay athhay idhay imselfhay amongay esethay eestray
Otay ebay onsortedcay ithway ethay umoroushay ightnay.
Indblay isay ishay ovelay, anday estbay efitsbay ethay arkday.

ERCUTIOmay.
Ifay ovelay ebay indblay, ovelay annotcay ithay ethay arkmay.
Ownay illway ehay itsay underay aay edlarmay eetray,
Anday ishway ishay istressmay ereway atthay indkay ofay uitfray
Asay aidsmay allcay edlarsmay enwhay eythay aughlay aloneay.
Oay Omeoray, atthay eshay ereway, Oay atthay eshay ereway
Anay open-arseay anday outhay aay operinpay earpay!
Omeoray, oodgay ightnay. I’llay otay myay uckle-bedtray.
Isthay ield-bedfay isay ootay oldcay orfay emay otay eepslay.
Omecay, allshay eway ogay?

ENVOLIObay.
Ogay enthay; orfay is’tay inay ainvay
Otay eeksay imhay erehay atthay eansmay otnay otay ebay oundfay.

exEunt._[_ay]

ENEScay Iiay. Apulet’scay Ardengay.

Enteray Omeoray.

OMEOray.
Ehay estsjay atay arsscay atthay evernay eltfay aay oundway.

Ulietjay appearsay aboveay atay aay indowway.

Utbay oftsay, atwhay ightlay oughthray onderyay indowway eaksbray?
Itay isay ethay eastay, anday Ulietjay isay ethay unsay!
Ariseay airfay unsay anday illkay ethay enviousay oonmay,
Owhay isay alreadyay icksay anday alepay ithway iefgray,
Atthay outhay erhay aidmay artay arfay oremay airfay anthay eshay.
Ebay otnay erhay aidmay incesay eshay isay enviousay;
Erhay estalvay iverylay isay utbay icksay anday eengray,
Anday onenay utbay oolsfay oday earway itay; astcay itay offay.
Itay isay myay adylay, Oay itay isay myay ovelay!
Oay, atthay eshay ewknay eshay ereway!
Eshay eaksspay, etyay eshay ayssay othingnay. Atwhay ofay atthay?
Erhay eyeay iscoursesday, Iay illway answeray itay.
Iay amay ootay oldbay, is’tay otnay otay emay eshay eaksspay.
Otway ofay ethay airestfay arsstay inay allay ethay eavenhay,
Avinghay omesay usinessbay, oday entreatay erhay eyesay
Otay inkletway inay eirthay eressphay illtay eythay eturnray.
Atwhay ifay erhay eyesay ereway erethay, eythay inay erhay eadhay?
Ethay ightnessbray ofay erhay eekchay ouldway ameshay osethay arsstay,
Asay aylightday othday aay amplay; erhay eyesay inay eavenhay
Ouldway oughthray ethay airyay egionray eamstray osay ightbray
Atthay irdsbay ouldway ingsay anday inkthay itay ereway otnay ightnay.
Eesay owhay eshay eanslay erhay eekchay uponay erhay andhay.
Oay atthay Iay ereway aay oveglay uponay atthay andhay,
Atthay Iay ightmay ouchtay atthay eekchay.

ULIETjay.
Ayay emay.

OMEOray.
Eshay eaksspay.
Oay eakspay againay ightbray angelay, orfay outhay artay
Asay oriousglay otay isthay ightnay, eingbay o’eray myay eadhay,
Asay isay aay ingedway essengermay ofay eavenhay
Untoay ethay ite-upturnedwhay onderingway eyesay
Ofay ortalsmay atthay allfay ackbay otay azegay onay imhay
Enwhay ehay estridesbay ethay azy-puffinglay oudsclay
Anday ailssay uponay ethay osombay ofay ethay airay.

ULIETjay.
Oay Omeoray, Omeoray, ereforewhay artay outhay Omeoray?
Enyday thyay atherfay anday efuseray thyay amenay.
Oray ifay outhay iltway otnay, ebay utbay ornsway myay ovelay,
Anday I’llay onay ongerlay ebay aay Apuletcay.

OMEOray.
asIde._[_ay] Allshay Iay earhay oremay, oray allshay Iay eakspay atay isthay?

ULIETjay.
iS’tay utbay thyay amenay atthay isay myay enemyay;
Outhay artay elfthysay, oughthay otnay aay Ontaguemay.
At’swhay Ontaguemay? Itay isay ornay andhay ornay ootfay,
Ornay armay, ornay acefay, ornay anyay otheray artpay
Elongingbay otay aay anmay. Oay ebay omesay otheray amenay.
At’swhay inay aay amenay? Atthay ichwhay eway allcay aay oseray
Byay anyay otheray amenay ouldway ellsmay asay eetsway;
Osay Omeoray ouldway, ereway ehay otnay Omeoray all’dcay,
Etainray atthay earday erfectionpay ichwhay ehay owesay
Ithoutway atthay itletay. Omeoray, offday thyay amenay,
Anday orfay thyay amenay, ichwhay isay onay artpay ofay eethay,
Aketay allay elfmysay.

OMEOray.
Iay aketay eethay atay thyay ordway.
Allcay emay utbay ovelay, anday I’llay ebay ewnay aptis’dbay;
Enceforthhay Iay evernay illway ebay Omeoray.

ULIETjay.
Atwhay anmay artay outhay atthay, usthay escreen’dbay inay ightnay
Osay umbleststay onay myay ounselcay?

OMEOray.
Byay aay amenay
Iay owknay otnay owhay otay elltay eethay owhay Iay amay:
Myay amenay, earday aintsay, isay atefulhay otay elfmysay,
Ecausebay itay isay anay enemyay otay eethay.
Adhay Iay itay ittenwray, Iay ouldway eartay ethay ordway.

ULIETjay.
Myay earsay avehay etyay otnay unkdray aay undredhay ordsway
Ofay thyay ongue’stay utteranceay, etyay Iay owknay ethay oundsay.
Artay outhay otnay Omeoray, anday aay Ontaguemay?

OMEOray.
Eithernay, airfay aidmay, ifay eitheray eethay islikeday.

ULIETjay.
Owhay am’stcay outhay itherhay, elltay emay, anday ereforewhay?
Ethay orcharday allsway areay ighhay anday ardhay otay imbclay,
Anday ethay aceplay eathday, onsideringcay owhay outhay artay,
Ifay anyay ofay myay insmenkay indfay eethay erehay.

OMEOray.
Ithway ove’slay ightlay ingsway idday Iay o’erperchay esethay allsway,
Orfay onystay imitslay annotcay oldhay ovelay outay,
Anday atwhay ovelay ancay oday, atthay aresday ovelay attemptay:
Ereforethay thyay insmenkay areay onay opstay otay emay.

ULIETjay.
Ifay eythay oday eesay eethay, eythay illway urdermay eethay.

OMEOray.
Alackay, erethay ieslay oremay erilpay inay inethay eyeay
Anthay entytway ofay eirthay ordssway. Ooklay outhay utbay eetsway,
Anday Iay amay oofpray againstay eirthay enmityay.

ULIETjay.
Iay ouldway otnay orfay ethay orldway eythay awsay eethay erehay.

OMEOray.
Iay avehay ight’snay oakclay otay idehay emay omfray eirthay eyesay,
Anday utbay outhay ovelay emay, etlay emthay indfay emay erehay.
Myay ifelay ereway etterbay endeday byay eirthay atehay
Anthay eathday oroguedpray, antingway ofay thyay ovelay.

ULIETjay.
Byay osewhay irectionday ound’stfay outhay outay isthay aceplay?

OMEOray.
Byay ovelay, atthay irstfay idday omptpray emay otay enquireay;
Ehay entlay emay ounselcay, anday Iay entlay imhay eyesay.
Iay amay onay ilotpay; etyay ertway outhay asay arfay
Asay atthay astvay oreshay ash’dway ithway ethay arthestfay easay,
Iay ouldshay adventureay orfay uchsay erchandisemay.

ULIETjay.
Outhay owestknay ethay askmay ofay ightnay isay onay myay acefay,
Elseay ouldway aay aidenmay ushblay epaintbay myay eekchay
Orfay atthay ichwhay outhay asthay eardhay emay eakspay onighttay.
Ainfay ouldway Iay elldway onay ormfay, ainfay, ainfay enyday
Atwhay Iay avehay okespay; utbay arewellfay omplimentcay.
Ostday outhay ovelay emay? Iay owknay outhay iltway aysay Ayay,
Anday Iay illway aketay thyay ordway. Etyay, ifay outhay ear’stsway,
Outhay aystmay ovepray alsefay. Atay overslay’ erjuriespay,
Eythay aysay Ovejay aughslay. Oay entlegay Omeoray,
Ifay outhay ostday ovelay, onouncepray itay aithfullyfay.
Oray ifay outhay inkestthay Iay amay ootay uicklyqay onway,
I’llay ownfray anday ebay erversepay, anday aysay eethay aynay,
Osay outhay iltway ooway. Utbay elseay, otnay orfay ethay orldway.
Inay uthtray, airfay Ontaguemay, Iay amay ootay ondfay;
Anday ereforethay outhay aystmay inkthay myay aviour’hay ightlay:
Utbay usttray emay, entlemangay, I’llay ovepray oremay uetray
Anthay osethay atthay avehay oremay unningcay otay ebay angestray.
Iay ouldshay avehay eenbay oremay angestray, Iay ustmay onfesscay,
Utbay atthay outhay overheard’stay, ereay Iay asway are’way,
Myay ue-lovetray assionpay; ereforethay ardonpay emay,
Anday otnay imputeay isthay ieldingyay otay ightlay ovelay,
Ichwhay ethay arkday ightnay athhay osay iscoveredday.

OMEOray.
Adylay, byay onderyay essedblay oonmay Iay owvay,
Atthay ipstay ithway ilversay allay esethay uit-treefray ops,tay—

ULIETjay.
Oay earsway otnay byay ethay oonmay, inconstantth’ay oonmay,
Atthay onthlymay angeschay inay erhay ircledcay orbay,
Estlay atthay thyay ovelay ovepray ikewiselay ariablevay.

OMEOray.
Atwhay allshay Iay earsway byay?

ULIETjay.
Oday otnay earsway atay allay.
Oray ifay outhay iltway, earsway byay thyay aciousgray elfsay,
Ichwhay isay ethay odgay ofay myay idolatryay,
Anday I’llay elievebay eethay.

OMEOray.
Ifay myay eart’shay earday ove,lay—

ULIETjay.
Ellway, oday otnay earsway. Althoughay Iay oyjay inay eethay,
Iay avehay onay oyjay ofay isthay ontractcay onighttay;
Itay isay ootay ashray, ootay unadvis’day, ootay uddensay,
Ootay ikelay ethay ightninglay, ichwhay othday easecay otay ebay
Ereay oneay ancay aysay iT“ay ightens.lay” Eetsway, oodgay ightnay.
Isthay udbay ofay ovelay, byay ummer’ssay ipeningray eathbray,
Aymay ovepray aay eauteousbay owerflay enwhay extnay eway eetmay.
Oodgay ightnay, oodgay ightnay. Asay eetsway eposeray anday estray
Omecay otay thyay earthay asay atthay ithinway myay eastbray.

OMEOray.
Oay iltway outhay eavelay emay osay unsatisfieday?

ULIETjay.
Atwhay atisfactionsay anstcay outhay avehay onighttay?

OMEOray.
Exchangeth’ay ofay thyay ove’slay aithfulfay owvay orfay inemay.

ULIETjay.
Iay avegay eethay inemay eforebay outhay idstday equestray itay;
Anday etyay Iay ouldway itay ereway otay ivegay againay.

OMEOray.
Ould’stway outhay ithdrawway itay? Orfay atwhay urposepay, ovelay?

ULIETjay.
Utbay otay ebay ankfray anday ivegay itay eethay againay.
Anday etyay Iay ishway utbay orfay ethay ingthay Iay avehay;
Myay ountybay isay asay oundlessbay asay ethay easay,
Myay ovelay asay eepday; ethay oremay Iay ivegay otay eethay,
Ethay oremay Iay avehay, orfay othbay areay infiniteay.
Iay earhay omesay oisenay ithinway. Earday ovelay, adieuay.
urSe[_nay allscay ithin._way]
Anonay, oodgay Urse!—sWeetnay Ontaguemay ebay uetray.
Aystay utbay aay ittlelay, Iay illway omecay againay.

exIt._[_ay]

OMEOray.
Oay essedblay, essedblay ightnay. Iay amay afearday,
Eingbay inay ightnay, allay isthay isay utbay aay eamdray,
Ootay atteringflay eetsway otay ebay ubstantialsay.

Enteray Ulietjay aboveay.

ULIETjay.
Eethray ordsway, earday Omeoray, anday oodgay ightnay indeeday.
Ifay atthay thyay entbay ofay ovelay ebay onourablehay,
Thyay urposepay arriagemay, endsay emay ordway omorrowtay,
Byay oneay atthay I’llay ocurepray otay omecay otay eethay,
Erewhay anday atwhay imetay outhay iltway erformpay ethay iteray,
Anday allay myay ortunesfay atay thyay ootfay I’llay aylay
Anday ollowfay eethay myay ordlay oughoutthray ethay orldway.

URSEnay.
itHin._[_way] Adammay.

ULIETjay.
Iay omecay, anon.ay— Utbay ifay outhay eanestmay otnay ellway,
Iay oday eseechbay ee,thay—

URSEnay.
itHin._[_way] Adammay.

ULIETjay.
Byay anday byay Iay omecay—
Otay easecay thyay ifestray anday eavelay emay otay myay iefgray.
Omorrowtay illway Iay endsay.

OMEOray.
Osay ivethray myay oul,say—

ULIETjay.
Aay ousandthay imestay oodgay ightnay.

exIt._[_ay]

OMEOray.
Aay ousandthay imestay ethay orseway, otay antway thyay ightlay.
Ovelay oesgay owardtay ovelay asay oolboysschay omfray eirthay ooksbay,
Utbay ovelay omfray ovelay, owardstay oolschay ithway eavyhay ookslay.

etIring[_ray owly._slay]

E-enterray Ulietjay, aboveay.

ULIETjay.
Isthay! Omeoray, isthay! Oay orfay aay alconer’sfay oicevay
Otay urelay isthay assel-gentletay ackbay againay.
Ondagebay isay oarsehay anday aymay otnay eakspay alouday,
Elseay ouldway Iay eartay ethay avecay erewhay Echoay ieslay,
Anday akemay erhay airyay onguetay oremay oarsehay anthay inemay
Ithway epetitionray ofay myay Omeo’sray amenay.

OMEOray.
Itay isay myay oulsay atthay allscay uponay myay amenay.
Owhay ilver-sweetsay oundsay overslay’ onguestay byay ightnay,
Ikelay oftestsay usicmay otay attendingay earsay.

ULIETjay.
Omeoray.

OMEOray.
Myay earday?

ULIETjay.
Atwhay o’clockay omorrowtay
Allshay Iay endsay otay eethay?

OMEOray.
Byay ethay ourhay ofay inenay.

ULIETjay.
Iay illway otnay ailfay. iS’tay entytway earsyay illtay enthay.
Iay avehay orgotfay whyay Iay idday allcay eethay ackbay.

OMEOray.
Etlay emay andstay erehay illtay outhay ememberray itay.

ULIETjay.
Iay allshay orgetfay, otay avehay eethay illstay andstay erethay,
Ememberingray owhay Iay ovelay thyay ompanycay.

OMEOray.
Anday I’llay illstay aystay, otay avehay eethay illstay orgetfay,
Orgettingfay anyay otheray omehay utbay isthay.

ULIETjay.
iS’tay almostay orningmay; Iay ouldway avehay eethay onegay,
Anday etyay onay artherfay anthay aay anton’sway irdbay,
Atthay etslay itay ophay aay ittlelay omfray erhay andhay,
Ikelay aay oorpay isonerpray inay ishay istedtway esgyvay,
Anday ithway aay ilksay eadthray ucksplay itay ackbay againay,
Osay oving-jealouslay ofay ishay ibertylay.

OMEOray.
Iay ouldway Iay ereway thyay irdbay.

ULIETjay.
Eetsway, osay ouldway Iay:
Etyay Iay ouldshay illkay eethay ithway uchmay erishingchay.
Oodgay ightnay, oodgay ightnay. Artingpay isay uchsay eetsway orrowsay
Atthay Iay allshay aysay oodgay ightnay illtay itay ebay orrowmay.

exIt._[_ay]

OMEOray.
Eepslay elldway uponay inethay eyesay, eacepay inay thyay eastbray.
Ouldway Iay ereway eepslay anday eacepay, osay eetsway otay estray.
Encehay illway Iay otay myay ostlyghay Ire’ssay ellcay,
Ishay elphay otay avecray anday myay earday aphay otay elltay.

exIt._[_ay]

ENEScay IIiay. Iarfray Awrence’slay Ellcay.

Enteray Iarfray Awrencelay ithway aay asketbay.

IARFray AWRENCElay.
Ethay ey-ey’dgray ornmay ilessmay onay ethay owningfray ightnay,
Equeringchay ethay easternay oudsclay ithway eaksstray ofay ightlay;
Anday eckledflay arknessday ikelay aay unkarddray eelsray
Omfray orthfay ay’sday athwaypay, ademay byay Itan’stay ieryfay eelswhay
Ownay, ereay ethay unsay advanceay ishay urningbay eyeay,
Ethay ayday otay eerchay, anday ight’snay ankday ewday otay dryay,
Iay ustmay upfillay isthay osieray agecay ofay oursay
Ithway alefulbay eedsway anday ecious-juicedpray owersflay.
Ethay earthay at’sthay ature’snay othermay, isay erhay ombtay;
Atwhay isay erhay uryingbay avegray, atthay isay erhay ombway:
Anday omfray erhay ombway ildrenchay ofay iversday indkay
Eway uckingsay onay erhay aturalnay osombay indfay.
Anymay orfay anymay irtuesvay excellentay,
Onenay utbay orfay omesay, anday etyay allay ifferentday.
Oay, icklemay isay ethay owerfulpay acegray atthay ieslay
Inay antsplay, erbshay, onesstay, anday eirthay uetray ualitiesqay.
Orfay aughtnay osay ilevay atthay onay ethay earthay othday ivelay
Utbay otay ethay earthay omesay ecialspay oodgay othday ivegay;
Ornay aughtay osay oodgay utbay, ain’dstray omfray atthay airfay useay,
Evoltsray omfray uetray irthbay, umblingstay onay abuseay.
Irtuevay itselfay urnstay icevay eingbay isappliedmay,
Anday icevay ometime’ssay byay actionay ignifiedday.

Enteray Omeoray.

Ithinway ethay infantay indray ofay isthay eakway owerflay
Oisonpay athhay esidenceray, anday edicinemay owerpay:
Orfay isthay, eingbay eltsmay, ithway atthay artpay eerschay eachay artpay;
Eingbay astedtay, aysslay allay ensessay ithway ethay earthay.
Otway uchsay opposeday ingskay encampay emthay illstay
Inay anmay asay ellway asay erbs,—gracehay anday uderay illway;
Anday erewhay ethay orserway isay edominantpray,
Ullfay oonsay ethay ankercay eathday eatsay upay atthay antplay.

OMEOray.
Oodgay orrowmay, atherfay.

IARFray AWRENCElay.
Enedicitebay!
Atwhay earlyay onguetay osay eetsway alutethsay emay?
Oungyay onsay, itay arguesay aay istemper’dday eadhay
Osay oonsay otay idbay oodgay orrowmay otay thyay edbay.
Arecay eepskay ishay atchway inay everyay olday an’smay eyeay,
Anday erewhay arecay odgeslay eepslay illway evernay ielay;
Utbay erewhay unbruiseday outhyay ithway unstuff’day ainbray
Othday ouchcay ishay imbslay, erethay oldengay eepslay othday eignray.
Ereforethay thyay earlinessay othday emay assureay
Outhay artay uprous’day ithway omesay istemperatureday;
Oray ifay otnay osay, enthay erehay Iay ithay itay ightray,
Ouray Omeoray athhay otnay eenbay inay edbay onighttay.

OMEOray.
Atthay astlay isay uetray; ethay eetersway estray asway inemay.

IARFray AWRENCElay.
Odgay ardonpay insay. Astway outhay ithway Osalineray?

OMEOray.
Ithway Osalineray, myay ostlyghay atherfay? Onay.
Iay avehay orgotfay atthay amenay, anday atthay ame’snay oeway.

IARFray AWRENCElay.
At’sthay myay oodgay onsay. Utbay erewhay asthay outhay eenbay enthay?

OMEOray.
I’llay elltay eethay ereay outhay askay itay emay againay.
Iay avehay eenbay eastingfay ithway inemay enemyay,
Erewhay onay aay uddensay oneay athhay oundedway emay
At’sthay byay emay oundedway. Othbay ouray emediesray
Ithinway thyay elphay anday olyhay icphysay ieslay.
Iay earbay onay atredhay, essedblay anmay; orfay olay,
Myay intercessionay ikewiselay eadsstay myay oefay.

IARFray AWRENCElay.
Ebay ainplay, oodgay onsay, anday omelyhay inay thyay iftdray;
Iddlingray onfessioncay indsfay utbay iddlingray iftshray.

OMEOray.
Enthay ainlyplay owknay myay eart’shay earday ovelay isay etsay
Onay ethay airfay aughterday ofay ichray Apuletcay.
Asay inemay onay ershay, osay ershay isay etsay onay inemay;
Anday allay ombin’dcay, avesay atwhay outhay ustmay ombinecay
Byay olyhay arriagemay. Enwhay, anday erewhay, anday owhay
Eway etmay, eway oo’dway, anday ademay exchangeay ofay owvay,
I’llay elltay eethay asay eway asspay; utbay isthay Iay aypray,
Atthay outhay onsentcay otay arrymay usay odaytay.

IARFray AWRENCElay.
Olyhay Aintsay Ancisfray! Atwhay aay angechay isay erehay!
Isay Osalineray, atthay outhay idstday ovelay osay earday,
Osay oonsay orsakenfay? Oungyay en’smay ovelay enthay ieslay
Otnay ulytray inay eirthay eartshay, utbay inay eirthay eyesay.
Esujay Ariamay, atwhay aay ealday ofay inebray
Athhay ash’dway thyay allowsay eekschay orfay Osalineray!
Owhay uchmay altsay aterway ownthray awayay inay asteway,
Otay easonsay ovelay, atthay ofay itay othday otnay astetay.
Ethay unsay otnay etyay thyay ighssay omfray eavenhay earsclay,
Thyay olday oansgray etyay ingray inay inemay ancientay earsay.
Olay erehay uponay thyay eekchay ethay ainstay othday itsay
Ofay anay olday eartay atthay isay otnay ash’dway offay etyay.
Ifay ereay outhay astway elfthysay, anday esethay oesway inethay,
Outhay anday esethay oesway ereway allay orfay Osalineray,
Anday artay outhay ang’dchay? Onouncepray isthay entencesay enthay,
Omenway aymay allfay, enwhay ere’sthay onay engthstray inay enmay.

OMEOray.
Outhay idd’stchay emay oftay orfay ovinglay Osalineray.

IARFray AWRENCElay.
Orfay otingday, otnay orfay ovinglay, upilpay inemay.

OMEOray.
Anday ad’stbay emay urybay ovelay.

IARFray AWRENCElay.
Otnay inay aay avegray
Otay aylay oneay inay, anotheray outay otay avehay.

OMEOray.
Iay aypray eethay idechay emay otnay, erhay Iay ovelay ownay
Othday acegray orfay acegray anday ovelay orfay ovelay alloway.
Ethay otheray idday otnay osay.

IARFray AWRENCElay.
Oay, eshay ewknay ellway
Thyay ovelay idday eadray byay oteray, atthay ouldcay otnay ellspay.
Utbay omecay oungyay avererway, omecay ogay ithway emay,
Inay oneay espectray I’llay thyay assistantay ebay;
Orfay isthay allianceay aymay osay appyhay ovepray,
Otay urntay ouryay ouseholdshay’ ancourray otay urepay ovelay.

OMEOray.
Oay etlay usay encehay; Iay andstay onay uddensay astehay.

IARFray AWRENCElay.
Iselyway anday owslay; eythay umblestay atthay unray astfay.

exEunt._[_ay]

ENEScay Ivay. Aay Eetstray.

Enteray Envoliobay anday Ercutiomay.

ERCUTIOmay.
Erewhay ethay evilday ouldshay isthay Omeoray ebay? Amecay ehay otnay omehay onighttay?

ENVOLIObay.
Otnay otay ishay ather’sfay; Iay okespay ithway ishay anmay.

ERCUTIOmay.
Whyay, atthay amesay alepay ard-heartedhay enchway, atthay Osalineray, ormentstay imhay osay
atthay ehay illway uresay unray admay.

ENVOLIObay.
Alttybay, ethay insmankay otay olday Apuletcay, athhay entsay aay etterlay otay ishay ather’sfay
ousehay.

ERCUTIOmay.
Aay allengechay, onay myay ifelay.

ENVOLIObay.
Omeoray illway answeray itay.

ERCUTIOmay.
Anyay anmay atthay ancay itewray aymay answeray aay etterlay.

ENVOLIObay.
Aynay, ehay illway answeray ethay etter’slay astermay, owhay ehay aresday, eingbay aredday.

ERCUTIOmay.
Alasay oorpay Omeoray, ehay isay alreadyay eadday, abbedstay ithway aay itewhay ench’sway ackblay
eyeay; unray oughthray ethay earay ithway aay ovelay ongsay, ethay eryvay inpay ofay ishay earthay
eftclay ithway ethay indblay ow-boy’sbay utt-shaftbay. Anday isay ehay aay anmay otay encounteray
Alttybay?

ENVOLIObay.
Whyay, atwhay isay Alttybay?

ERCUTIOmay.
Oremay anthay Incepray ofay atscay. Oay, e’shay ethay ourageouscay aptaincay ofay
omplimentscay. Ehay ightsfay asay ouyay ingsay ick-songpray, eepskay imetay, istanceday,
anday oportionpray. Ehay estsray ishay inimmay estray, oneay, otway, anday ethay irdthay inay
ouryay osombay: ethay eryvay utcherbay ofay aay ilksay uttonbay, aay uellistday, aay uellistday;
aay entlemangay ofay ethay eryvay irstfay ousehay, ofay ethay irstfay anday econdsay ausecay. Ahay,
ethay immortalay assadopay, ethay untopay eversoray, ethay ayhay.

ENVOLIObay.
Ethay atwhay?

ERCUTIOmay.
Ethay oxpay ofay uchsay anticay ispinglay, affectingay antasiesphay; esethay ewnay unerstay
ofay accentay. Byay Esujay, aay eryvay oodgay adeblay, aay eryvay alltay anmay, aay eryvay oodgay
orewhay. Whyay, isay otnay isthay aay amentablelay ingthay, andsiregray, atthay eway ouldshay
ebay usthay afflicteday ithway esethay angestray iesflay, esethay ashion-mongersfay,
esethay ardon-me’spay, owhay andstay osay uchmay onay ethay ewnay ormfay atthay eythay annotcay
itsay atay easeay onay ethay olday enchbay? Oay eirthay onesbay, eirthay onesbay!

ULIETjay.
Ethay ockclay uckstray inenay enwhay Iay idday endsay ethay Ursenay,
Inay alfhay anay ourhay eshay omisedpray otay eturnray.
Erchancepay eshay annotcay eetmay imhay. At’sthay otnay osay.
Oay, eshay isay amelay. Ove’slay eraldshay ouldshay ebay oughtsthay,
Ichwhay entay imestay asterfay idesglay anthay ethay un’ssay eamsbay,
Ivingdray ackbay adowsshay overay oweringlay illshay:
Ereforethay oday imble-pinion’dnay ovesday awdray ovelay,
Anday ereforethay athhay ethay ind-swiftway Upidcay ingsway.
Ownay isay ethay unsay uponay ethay ighmosthay illhay
Ofay isthay ay’sday ourneyjay, anday omfray inenay illtay elvetway
Isay eethray onglay ourshay, etyay eshay isay otnay omecay.
Adhay eshay affectionsay anday armway outhfulyay oodblay,
E’dshay ebay asay iftsway inay otionmay asay aay allbay;
Myay ordsway ouldway andybay erhay otay myay eetsway ovelay,
Anday ishay otay emay.
Utbay olday olksfay, anymay eignfay asay eythay ereway eadday;
Unwieldyay, owslay, eavyhay anday alepay asay eadlay.

Itay isay enoughay Iay aymay utbay allcay erhay inemay.

IARFray AWRENCElay.
Esethay iolentvay elightsday avehay iolentvay endsay,

Isay oathsomelay inay ishay ownay eliciousnessday,
