ACtay Vay

ENEScay Iay. Antuamay. Aay Eetstray.


Enteray Omeoray.

OMEOray.
Ifay Iay aymay usttray ethay atteringflay eyeay ofay eepslay,
Myay eamsdray esagepray omesay oyfuljay ewsnay atay andhay.
Myay osom’sbay ordlay itssay ightlylay inay ishay onethray;
Anday allay isthay ayday anay unaccustom’day iritspay
Iftslay emay aboveay ethay oundgray ithway eerfulchay oughtsthay.
Iay eamtdray myay adylay amecay anday oundfay emay ead,day—
Angestray eamdray, atthay ivesgay aay eadday anmay eavelay otay ink!thay—
Anday eath’dbray uchsay ifelay ithway isseskay inay myay ipslay,
Atthay Iay eviv’dray, anday asway anay emperoray.
Ahay emay, owhay eetsway isay ovelay itselfay ossess’dpay,
Enwhay utbay ove’slay adowsshay areay osay ichray inay oyjay.

Enteray Althasarbay.

Ewsnay omfray Eronavay! Owhay ownay, Althasarbay?
Ostday outhay otnay ingbray emay etterslay omfray ethay Iarfray?
Owhay othday myay adylay? Isay myay atherfay ellway?
Owhay aresfay myay Ulietjay? Atthay Iay askay againay;
Orfay othingnay ancay ebay illay ifay eshay ebay ellway.

ALTHASARbay.
Enthay eshay isay ellway, anday othingnay ancay ebay illay.
Erhay odybay eepsslay inay Apel’scay onumentmay,
Anday erhay immortalay artpay ithway angelsay iveslay.
Iay awsay erhay aidlay owlay inay erhay indred’skay aultvay,
Anday esentlypray ooktay ostpay otay elltay itay ouyay.
Oay ardonpay emay orfay ingingbray esethay illay ewsnay,
Incesay ouyay idday eavelay itay orfay myay officeay, irsay.

OMEOray.
Isay itay evenay osay? Enthay Iay efyday ouyay, arsstay!
Outhay ow’stknay myay odginglay. Etgay emay inkay anday aperpay,
Anday irehay ost-horsespay. Iay illway encehay onighttay.

ALTHASARbay.
Iay oday eseechbay ouyay irsay, avehay atiencepay.
Ouryay ookslay areay alepay anday ildway, anday oday importay
Omesay isadventuremay.

OMEOray.
Ushtay, outhay artay eceiv’dday.
Eavelay emay, anday oday ethay ingthay Iay idbay eethay oday.
Asthay outhay onay etterslay otay emay omfray ethay Iarfray?

ALTHASARbay.
Onay, myay oodgay ordlay.

OMEOray.
Onay attermay. Etgay eethay onegay,
Anday irehay osethay orseshay. I’llay ebay ithway eethay aightstray.

exIt[_ay Althasar._bay]

Ellway, Ulietjay, Iay illway ielay ithway eethay onighttay.
Et’slay eesay orfay eansmay. Oay ischiefmay outhay artay iftsway
Otay enteray inay ethay oughtsthay ofay esperateday enmay.
Iay oday ememberray anay apothecary,ay—
Anday ereaboutshay ehay ells,—whichdway atelay Iay otednay
Inay atter’dtay eedsway, ithway overwhelmingay owsbray,
Ullingcay ofay implessay, eagremay ereway ishay ookslay,
Arpshay iserymay adhay ornway imhay otay ethay onesbay;
Anday inay ishay eedynay opshay aay ortoisetay unghay,
Anay alligatoray uff’dstay, anday otheray insskay
Ofay ill-shapeday ishesfay; anday aboutay ishay elvesshay
Aay eggarlybay accountay ofay emptyay oxesbay,
Eengray earthenay otspay, addersblay, anday ustymay eedssay,
Emnantsray ofay ackthreadpay, anday olday akescay ofay osesray
Ereway inlythay atter’dscay, otay akemay upay aay owshay.
Otingnay isthay enurypay, otay elfmysay Iay aidsay,
Anday ifay aay anmay idday eednay aay oisonpay ownay,
Osewhay alesay isay esentpray eathday inay Antuamay,
Erehay iveslay aay aitiffcay etchwray ouldway ellsay itay imhay.
Oay, isthay amesay oughtthay idday utbay orerunfay myay eednay,
Anday isthay amesay eedynay anmay ustmay ellsay itay emay.
Asay Iay ememberray, isthay ouldshay ebay ethay ousehay.
Eingbay olidayhay, ethay eggar’sbay opshay isay utshay.
Atwhay, ohay! Apothecaryay!

Enteray Apothecaryay.

APOTHECARyay.
Owhay allscay osay oudlay?

OMEOray.
Omecay itherhay, anmay. Iay eesay atthay outhay artay oorpay.
Oldhay, erethay isay ortyfay ucatsday. Etlay emay avehay
Aay amdray ofay oisonpay, uchsay oon-speedingsay eargay
Asay illway isperseday itselfay oughthray allay ethay einsvay,
Atthay ethay ife-wearylay akertay aymay allfay eadday,
Anday atthay ethay unktray aymay ebay ischarg’dday ofay eathbray
Asay iolentlyvay asay astyhay owderpay ir’dfay
Othday urryhay omfray ethay atalfay annon’scay ombway.

APOTHECARyay.
Uchsay ortalmay ugsdray Iay avehay, utbay Antua’smay awlay
Isay eathday otay anyay ehay atthay uttersay emthay.

OMEOray.
Artay outhay osay arebay anday ullfay ofay etchednesswray,
Anday ear’stfay otay ieday? Aminefay isay inay thyay eekschay,
Eednay anday oppressionay arvethstay inay inethay eyesay,
Ontemptcay anday eggarybay angshay uponay thyay ackbay.
Ethay orldway isay otnay thyay iendfray, ornay ethay orld’sway awlay;
Ethay orldway affordsay onay awlay otay akemay eethay ichray;
Enthay ebay otnay oorpay, utbay eakbray itay anday aketay isthay.

APOTHECARyay.
Myay overtypay, utbay otnay myay illway onsentscay.

OMEOray.
Iay aypay thyay overtypay, anday otnay thyay illway.

APOTHECARyay.
Utpay isthay inay anyay iquidlay ingthay ouyay illway
Anday inkdray itay offay; anday, ifay ouyay adhay ethay engthstray
Ofay entytway enmay, itay ouldway espatchday ouyay aightstray.

OMEOray.
Erethay isay thyay oldgay, orseway oisonpay otay en’smay oulssay,
Oingday oremay urdermay inay isthay oathsomelay orldway
Anthay esethay oorpay ompoundscay atthay outhay aystmay otnay ellsay.
Iay ellsay eethay oisonpay, outhay asthay oldsay emay onenay.
Arewellfay, uybay oodfay, anday etgay elfthysay inay eshflay.
Omecay, ordialcay anday otnay oisonpay, ogay ithway emay
Otay Uliet’sjay avegray, orfay erethay ustmay Iay useay eethay.

exEunt._[_ay]

ENEScay Iiay. Iarfray Awrence’slay Ellcay.

Enteray Iarfray Ohnjay.

IARFray OHNjay.
Olyhay Anciscanfray Iarfray! Otherbray, ohay!

Enteray Iarfray Awrencelay.

IARFray AWRENCElay.
Isthay amesay ouldshay ebay ethay oicevay ofay Iarfray Ohnjay.
Elcomeway omfray Antuamay. Atwhay ayssay Omeoray?
Oray, ifay ishay indmay ebay itwray, ivegay emay ishay etterlay.

IARFray OHNjay.
Oinggay otay indfay aay arefootbay otherbray outay,
Oneay ofay ouray orderay, otay associateay emay,
Erehay inay isthay itycay isitingvay ethay icksay,
Anday indingfay imhay, ethay earcherssay ofay ethay owntay,
Uspectingsay atthay eway othbay ereway inay aay ousehay
Erewhay ethay infectiousay estilencepay idday eignray,
Eal’dsay upay ethay oorsday, anday ouldway otnay etlay usay orthfay,
Osay atthay myay eedspay otay Antuamay erethay asway ay’dstay.

IARFray AWRENCElay.
Owhay arebay myay etterlay enthay otay Omeoray?

IARFray OHNjay.
Iay ouldcay otnay endsay it,—hereay itay isay again,ay—
Ornay etgay aay essengermay otay ingbray itay eethay,
Osay earfulfay ereway eythay ofay infectionay.

IARFray AWRENCElay.
Unhappyay ortunefay! Byay myay otherhoodbray,
Ethay etterlay asway otnay icenay, utbay ullfay ofay argechay,
Ofay earday importay, anday ethay eglectingnay itay
Aymay oday uchmay angerday. Iarfray Ohnjay, ogay encehay,
Etgay emay anay ironay owcray anday ingbray itay aightstray
Untoay myay ellcay.

IARFray OHNjay.
Otherbray, I’llay ogay anday ingbray itay eethay.

exIt._[_ay]

IARFray AWRENCElay.
Ownay ustmay Iay otay ethay onumentmay aloneay.
Ithinway isthay eethray ourshay illway airfay Ulietjay akeway.
Eshay illway eshrewbay emay uchmay atthay Omeoray
Athhay adhay onay oticenay ofay esethay accidentsay;
Utbay Iay illway itewray againay otay Antuamay,
Anday eepkay erhay atay myay ellcay illtay Omeoray omecay.
Oorpay ivinglay orsecay, os’dclay inay aay eadday an’smay ombtay.

exIt._[_ay]

ENEScay IIiay. Aay urchyardchay; inay itay aay Onumentmay elongingbay otay ethay Apuletscay.

Enteray Arispay, anday ishay Agepay earingbay owersflay anday aay orchtay.

ARISpay.
Ivegay emay thyay orchtay, oybay. Encehay anday andstay aloofay.
Etyay utpay itay outay, orfay Iay ouldway otnay ebay eensay.
Underay ondyay ewyay eetray aylay eethay allay alongay,
Oldinghay thyay earay oseclay otay ethay ollowhay oundgray;
Osay allshay onay ootfay uponay ethay urchyardchay eadtray,
Eingbay ooselay, unfirmay, ithway iggingday upay ofay avesgray,
Utbay outhay altshay earhay itay. Istlewhay enthay otay emay,
Asay ignalsay atthay outhay ear’sthay omethingsay approachay.
Ivegay emay osethay owersflay. Oday asay Iay idbay eethay, ogay.

AGEpay.
asIde._[_ay] Iay amay almostay afraiday otay andstay aloneay
Erehay inay ethay urchyardchay; etyay Iay illway adventureay.

etIres._[_ray]

ARISpay.
Eetsway owerflay, ithway owersflay thyay idalbray edbay Iay ewstray.
Oay oeway, thyay anopycay isay ustday anday onesstay,
Ichwhay ithway eetsway aterway ightlynay Iay illway ewday,
Oray antingway atthay, ithway earstay istill’dday byay oansmay.
Ethay obsequiesay atthay Iay orfay eethay illway eepkay,
Ightlynay allshay ebay otay ewstray thyay avegray anday eepway.

e[_thay Agepay istles._whay]

Ethay oybay ivesgay arningway omethingsay othday approachay.
Atwhay ursedcay ootfay andersway isthay ayway onighttay,
Otay osscray myay obsequiesay anday uetray ove’slay iteray?
Atwhay, ithway aay orchtay! Ufflemay emay, ightnay, awhileay.

etIres._[_ray]

Enteray Omeoray anday Althasarbay ithway aay orchtay, attockmay, &cay.

OMEOray.
Ivegay emay atthay attockmay anday ethay enchingwray ironay.
Oldhay, aketay isthay etterlay; earlyay inay ethay orningmay
Eesay outhay eliverday itay otay myay ordlay anday atherfay.
Ivegay emay ethay ightlay; uponay thyay ifelay Iay argechay eethay,
Ate’erwhay outhay ear’sthay oray eestsay, andstay allay aloofay
Anday oday otnay interruptay emay inay myay oursecay.
Whyay Iay escendday intoay isthay edbay ofay eathday
Isay artlypay otay eholdbay myay ady’slay acefay,
Utbay ieflychay otay aketay encethay omfray erhay eadday ingerfay
Aay eciouspray ingray, aay ingray atthay Iay ustmay useay
Inay earday employmentay. Ereforethay encehay, ebay onegay.
Utbay ifay outhay ealousjay ostday eturnray otay pryay
Inay atwhay Iay urtherfay allshay intenday otay oday,
Byay eavenhay Iay illway eartay eethay ointjay byay ointjay,
Anday ewstray isthay ungryhay urchyardchay ithway thyay imbslay.
Ethay imetay anday myay intentsay areay avage-wildsay;
Oremay iercefay anday oremay inexorableay arfay
Anthay emptyay igerstay oray ethay oaringray easay.

ALTHASARbay.
Iay illway ebay onegay, irsay, anday otnay oubletray ouyay.

OMEOray.
Osay altshay outhay owshay emay iendshipfray. Aketay outhay atthay.
Ivelay, anday ebay osperouspray, anday arewellfay, oodgay ellowfay.

ALTHASARbay.
Orfay allay isthay amesay, I’llay idehay emay ereabouthay.
Ishay ookslay Iay earfay, anday ishay intentsay Iay oubtday.

etIres_[_ray]

OMEOray.
Outhay etestableday awmay, outhay ombway ofay eathday,
Org’dgay ithway ethay earestday orselmay ofay ethay earthay,
Usthay Iay enforceay thyay ottenray awsjay otay openay,

eaKing[_bray openay ethay oorday ofay ethay onument._may]

Anday inay espiteday, I’llay amcray eethay ithway oremay oodfay.

ARISpay.
Isthay isay atthay anish’dbay aughtyhay Ontaguemay
Atthay urder’dmay myay ove’slay ousin,—withcay ichwhay iefgray,
Itay isay upposedsay, ethay airfay eaturecray ied,day—
Anday erehay isay omecay otay oday omesay illainousvay ameshay
Otay ethay eadday odiesbay. Iay illway apprehenday imhay.

adVances._[_ay]

Opstay thyay unhallow’day oiltay, ilevay Ontaguemay.
Ancay engeancevay ebay ursu’dpay urtherfay anthay eathday?
Ondemnedcay illainvay, Iay oday apprehenday eethay.
Obeyay, anday ogay ithway emay, orfay outhay ustmay ieday.

OMEOray.
Iay ustmay indeeday; anday ereforethay amecay Iay itherhay.
Oodgay entlegay outhyay, empttay otnay aay esperateday anmay.
Flyay encehay anday eavelay emay. Inkthay uponay esethay onegay;
Etlay emthay affrightay eethay. Iay eseechbay eethay, outhyay,
Utpay otnay anotheray insay uponay myay eadhay
Byay urgingay emay otay uryfay. Oay ebay onegay.
Byay eavenhay Iay ovelay eethay etterbay anthay elfmysay;
Orfay Iay omecay itherhay arm’day againstay elfmysay.
Aystay otnay, ebay onegay, ivelay, anday ereafterhay aysay,
Aay adman’smay ercymay idbay eethay unray awayay.

ARISpay.
Iay oday efyday thyay onjurationcay,
Anday apprehenday eethay orfay aay elonfay erehay.

OMEOray.
Iltway outhay ovokepray emay? Enthay avehay atay eethay, oybay!

ey[_thay ight._fay]

AGEpay.
Oay ordlay, eythay ightfay! Iay illway ogay allcay ethay atchway.

exIt._[_ay]

ARISpay.
Oay, Iay amay ainslay! alLs._[_fay] Ifay outhay ebay ercifulmay,
Openay ethay ombtay, aylay emay ithway Ulietjay.

ieS._[_day]

OMEOray.
Inay aithfay, Iay illway. Etlay emay erusepay isthay acefay.
Ercutio’smay insmankay, oblenay Ountycay Arispay!
Atwhay aidsay myay anmay, enwhay myay etossedbay oulsay
Idday otnay attenday imhay asay eway oderay? Iay inkthay
Ehay oldtay emay Arispay ouldshay avehay arriedmay Ulietjay.
Aidsay ehay otnay osay? Oray idday Iay eamdray itay osay?
Oray amay Iay admay, earinghay imhay alktay ofay Ulietjay,
Otay inkthay itay asway osay? Oay, ivegay emay thyay andhay,
Oneay itwray ithway emay inay oursay isfortune’smay ookbay.
I’llay urybay eethay inay aay iumphanttray avegray.
Aay avegray? Oay onay, aay anternlay, aught’redslay outhyay,
Orfay erehay ieslay Ulietjay, anday erhay eautybay akesmay
Isthay aultvay aay eastingfay esencepray ullfay ofay ightlay.
Eathday, ielay outhay erethay, byay aay eadday anmay interr’day.

ayIng[_lay Arispay inay ethay onument._may]

Owhay oftay enwhay enmay areay atay ethay ointpay ofay eathday
Avehay eythay eenbay errymay! Ichwhay eirthay eeperskay allcay
Aay ightninglay eforebay eathday. Oay, owhay aymay Iay
Allcay isthay aay ightninglay? Oay myay ovelay, myay ifeway,
Eathday atthay athhay uck’dsay ethay oneyhay ofay thyay eathbray,
Athhay adhay onay owerpay etyay uponay thyay eautybay.
Outhay artay otnay onquer’dcay. Eauty’sbay ensignay etyay
Isay imsoncray inay thyay ipslay anday inay thyay eekschay,
Anday eath’sday alepay agflay isay otnay advanceday erethay.
Alttybay, iestlay outhay erethay inay thyay oodyblay eetshay?
Oay, atwhay oremay avourfay ancay Iay oday otay eethay
Anthay ithway atthay andhay atthay utcay thyay outhyay inay aintway
Otay undersay ishay atthay asway inethay enemyay?
Orgivefay emay, ousincay. Ahay, earday Ulietjay,
Whyay artay outhay etyay osay airfay? Allshay Iay elievebay
Atthay unsubstantialay eathday isay amorousay;
Anday atthay ethay eanlay abhorreday onstermay eepskay
Eethay erehay inay arkday otay ebay ishay aramourpay?
Orfay earfay ofay atthay Iay illstay illway aystay ithway eethay,
Anday evernay omfray isthay alacepay ofay imday ightnay
Epartday againay. Erehay, erehay illway Iay emainray
Ithway ormsway atthay areay thyay ambermaidschay. Oay, erehay
Illway Iay etsay upay myay everlastingay estray;
Anday akeshay ethay okeyay ofay inauspiciousay arsstay
Omfray isthay orld-weariedway eshflay. Eyesay, ooklay ouryay astlay.
Armsay, aketay ouryay astlay embraceay! Anday, ipslay, Oay ouyay
Ethay oorsday ofay eathbray, ealsay ithway aay ighteousray isskay
Aay atelessday argainbay otay engrossingay eathday.
Omecay, itterbay onductcay, omecay, unsavouryay uidegay.
Outhay esperateday ilotpay, ownay atay onceay unray onay
Ethay ashingday ocksray thyay ea-sicksay earyway arkbay.
Ere’shay otay myay ovelay! inKs._[_dray] Oay uetray apothecaryay!
Thyay ugsdray areay uickqay. Usthay ithway aay isskay Iay ieday.

ieS._[_day]

Enteray, atay ethay otheray enday ofay ethay Urchyardchay, Iarfray Awrencelay, ithway aay
anternlay, owcray, anday adespay.

IARFray AWRENCElay.
Aintsay Ancisfray ebay myay eedspay. Owhay oftay onighttay
Avehay myay olday eetfay umbledstay atay avesgray? O’swhay erethay?
Owhay isay itay atthay onsortscay, osay atelay, ethay eadday?

ALTHASARbay.
Ere’shay oneay, aay iendfray, anday oneay atthay owsknay ouyay ellway.

IARFray AWRENCElay.
Issblay ebay uponay ouyay. Elltay emay, oodgay myay iendfray,
Atwhay orchtay isay ondyay atthay ainlyvay endslay ishay ightlay
Otay ubsgray anday eyelessay ullsskay? Asay Iay iscernday,
Itay urnethbay inay ethay Apelscay’ onumentmay.

ALTHASARbay.
Itay othday osay, olyhay irsay, anday ere’sthay myay astermay,
Oneay atthay ouyay ovelay.

IARFray AWRENCElay.
Owhay isay itay?

ALTHASARbay.
Omeoray.

IARFray AWRENCElay.
Owhay onglay athhay ehay eenbay erethay?

ALTHASARbay.
Ullfay alfhay anay ourhay.

IARFray AWRENCElay.
Ogay ithway emay otay ethay aultvay.

ALTHASARbay.
Iay areday otnay, irsay;
Myay astermay owsknay otnay utbay Iay amay onegay encehay,
Anday earfullyfay idday enacemay emay ithway eathday
Ifay Iay idday aystay otay ooklay onay ishay intentsay.

IARFray AWRENCElay.
Aystay enthay, I’llay ogay aloneay. Earfay omescay uponay emay.
Oay, uchmay Iay earfay omesay illay unluckyay ingthay.

ALTHASARbay.
Asay Iay idday eepslay underay isthay ewyay eetray erehay,
Iay eamtdray myay astermay anday anotheray oughtfay,
Anday atthay myay astermay ewslay imhay.

IARFray AWRENCElay.
Omeoray! adVances._[_ay]
Alackay, alackay, atwhay oodblay isay isthay ichwhay ainsstay
Ethay onystay entranceay ofay isthay epulchresay?
Atwhay eanmay esethay asterlessmay anday orygay ordssway
Otay ielay iscolour’dday byay isthay aceplay ofay eacepay?

enTers[_ay ethay onument._may]

Omeoray! Oay, alepay! Owhay elseay? Atwhay, Arispay ootay?
Anday eep’dstay inay oodblay? Ahay atwhay anay unkinday ourhay
Isay uiltygay ofay isthay amentablelay ancechay?
Ethay adylay irsstay.

ulIet[_jay akesway anday irs._stay]

ULIETjay.
Oay omfortablecay Iarfray, erewhay isay myay ordlay?
Iay oday ememberray ellway erewhay Iay ouldshay ebay,
Anday erethay Iay amay. Erewhay isay myay Omeoray?

oiSe[_nay ithin._way]

IARFray AWRENCElay.
Iay earhay omesay oisenay. Adylay, omecay omfray atthay estnay
Ofay eathday, ontagioncay, anday unnaturalay eepslay.
Aay eatergray owerpay anthay eway ancay ontradictcay
Athhay artedthway ouray intentsay. Omecay, omecay awayay.
Thyay usbandhay inay thyay osombay erethay ieslay eadday;
Anday Arispay ootay. Omecay, I’llay isposeday ofay eethay
Amongay aay isterhoodsay ofay olyhay unsnay.
Aystay otnay otay uestionqay, orfay ethay atchway isay omingcay.
Omecay, ogay, oodgay Ulietjay. Iay areday onay ongerlay aystay.

ULIETjay.
Ogay, etgay eethay encehay, orfay Iay illway otnay awayay.

exIt[_ay Iarfray Awrence._lay]

At’swhay erehay? Aay upcay os’dclay inay myay uetray ove’slay andhay?
Oisonpay, Iay eesay, athhay eenbay ishay imelesstay enday.
Oay urlchay. Inkdray allay, anday eftlay onay iendlyfray opdray
Otay elphay emay afteray? Iay illway isskay thyay ipslay.
Aplyhay omesay oisonpay etyay othday anghay onay emthay,
Otay akemay emay ieday ithway aay estorativeray.

isSes[_kay im._hay]

Thyay ipslay areay armway!

IRSTfay ATCHway.
itHin._[_way] Eadlay, oybay. Ichwhay ayway?

ULIETjay.
Eayay, oisenay? Enthay I’llay ebay iefbray. Oay appyhay aggerday.

atChing[_snay Omeo’sray agger._day]

Isthay isay thyay eathshay. abs[_stay erself_hay] Erethay estray, anday etlay emay ieday.

alLs[_fay onay Omeo’sray odybay anday ies._day]

Enteray Atchway ithway ethay Agepay ofay Arispay.

AGEpay.
Isthay isay ethay aceplay. Erethay, erewhay ethay orchtay othday urnbay.

IRSTfay ATCHway.
Ethay oundgray isay oodyblay. Earchsay aboutay ethay urchyardchay.
Ogay, omesay ofay ouyay, oe’erwhay ouyay indfay attachay.

exEunt[_ay omesay ofay ethay Atch._way]

Itifulpay ightsay! Erehay ieslay ethay Ountycay ainslay,
Anday Ulietjay eedingblay, armway, anday ewlynay eadday,
Owhay erehay athhay ainlay isthay otway aysday uriedbay.
Ogay elltay ethay Incepray; unray otay ethay Apuletscay.
Aiseray upay ethay Ontaguesmay, omesay othersay earchsay.

exEunt[_ay othersay ofay ethay Atch._way]

Eway eesay ethay oundgray ereonwhay esethay oesway oday ielay,
Utbay ethay uetray oundgray ofay allay esethay iteouspay oesway
Eway annotcay ithoutway ircumstancecay escryday.

E-enterray omesay ofay ethay Atchway ithway Althasarbay.

ECONDsay ATCHway.
Ere’shay Omeo’sray anmay. Eway oundfay imhay inay ethay urchyardchay.

IRSTfay ATCHway.
Oldhay imhay inay afetysay illtay ethay Incepray omecay itherhay.

E-enterray othersay ofay ethay Atchway ithway Iarfray Awrencelay.

IRDThay ATCHway. Erehay isay aay Iarfray atthay emblestray, ighssay, anday eepsway.
Eway ooktay isthay attockmay anday isthay adespay omfray imhay
Asay ehay asway omingcay omfray isthay urchyardchay idesay.

IRSTfay ATCHway.
Aay eatgray uspicionsay. Aystay ethay Iarfray ootay.

Enteray ethay Incepray anday Attendantsay.

INCEPray.
Atwhay isadventuremay isay osay earlyay upay,
Atthay allscay ouray ersonpay omfray ouray orning’smay estray?

Enteray Apuletcay, Adylay Apuletcay anday othersay.

APULETcay.
Atwhay ouldshay itay ebay atthay eythay osay iekshray abroaday?

ADYlay APULETcay.
Oay ethay eoplepay inay ethay eetstray cryay Omeoray,
Omesay Ulietjay, anday omesay Arispay, anday allay unray
Ithway openay outcryay owardtay ouray onumentmay.

INCEPray.
Atwhay earfay isay isthay ichwhay artlesstay inay ouray earsay?

IRSTfay ATCHway.
Overeignsay, erehay ieslay ethay Ountycay Arispay ainslay,
Anday Omeoray eadday, anday Ulietjay, eadday eforebay,
Armway anday ewnay ill’dkay.

INCEPray.
Earchsay, eeksay, anday owknay owhay isthay oulfay urdermay omescay.

IRSTfay ATCHway.
Erehay isay aay Iarfray, anday aughter’dslay Omeo’sray anmay,
Ithway instrumentsay uponay emthay itfay otay openay
Esethay eadday en’smay ombstay.

APULETcay.
Oay eavenhay! Oay ifeway, ooklay owhay ouray aughterday eedsblay!
Isthay aggerday athhay ista’enmay, orfay olay, ishay ousehay
Isay emptyay onay ethay ackbay ofay Ontaguemay,
Anday itay is-sheathedmay inay myay aughter’sday osombay.

ADYlay APULETcay.
Oay emay! Isthay ightsay ofay eathday isay asay aay ellbay
Atthay arnsway myay olday ageay otay aay epulchresay.

Enteray Ontaguemay anday othersay.

INCEPray.
Omecay, Ontaguemay, orfay outhay artay earlyay upay,
Otay eesay thyay onsay anday eirhay oremay earlyay ownday.

ONTAGUEmay.
Alasay, myay iegelay, myay ifeway isay eadday onighttay.
Iefgray ofay myay on’ssay exileay athhay opp’dstay erhay eathbray.
Atwhay urtherfay oeway onspirescay againstay inemay ageay?

INCEPray.
Ooklay, anday outhay altshay eesay.

ONTAGUEmay.
Oay outhay untaughtay! Atwhay annersmay isay inay isthay,
Otay esspray eforebay thyay atherfay otay aay avegray?

INCEPray.
Ealsay upay ethay outhmay ofay outrageay orfay aay ilewhay,
Illtay eway ancay earclay esethay ambiguitiesay,
Anday owknay eirthay ingspray, eirthay eadhay, eirthay uetray escentday,
Anday enthay illway Iay ebay eneralgay ofay ouryay oesway,
Anday eadlay ouyay evenay otay eathday. Eantimemay orbearfay,
Anday etlay ischancemay ebay aveslay otay atiencepay.
Ingbray orthfay ethay artiespay ofay uspicionsay.

IARFray AWRENCElay.
Iay amay ethay eatestgray, ableay otay oday eastlay,
Etyay ostmay uspectedsay, asay ethay imetay anday aceplay
Othday akemay againstay emay, ofay isthay irefulday urdermay.
Anday erehay Iay andstay, othbay otay impeachay anday urgepay
Elfmysay ondemnedcay anday elfmysay excus’day.

INCEPray.
Enthay aysay atay onceay atwhay outhay ostday owknay inay isthay.

IARFray AWRENCElay.
Iay illway ebay iefbray, orfay myay ortshay ateday ofay eathbray
Isay otnay osay onglay asay isay aay edioustay aletay.
Omeoray, erethay eadday, asway usbandhay otay atthay Ulietjay,
Anday eshay, erethay eadday, atthay Omeo’sray aithfulfay ifeway.
Iay arriedmay emthay; anday eirthay ol’nstay arriagemay ayday
Asway Alt’stybay oomsdayday, osewhay untimelyay eathday
Anish’dbay ethay ew-madenay idegroombray omfray isthay itycay;
Orfay omwhay, anday otnay orfay Alttybay, Ulietjay in’dpay.
Ouyay, otay emoveray atthay iegesay ofay iefgray omfray erhay,
Etroth’dbay, anday ouldway avehay arriedmay erhay erforcepay
Otay Ountycay Arispay. Enthay omescay eshay otay emay,
Anday ithway ildway ookslay, idbay emay eviseday omesay eansmay
Otay idray erhay omfray isthay econdsay arriagemay,
Oray inay myay ellcay erethay ouldway eshay illkay erselfhay.
Enthay avegay Iay erhay, osay utoredtay byay myay artay,
Aay eepingslay otionpay, ichwhay osay ooktay effectay
Asay Iay intendeday, orfay itay oughtwray onay erhay
Ethay ormfay ofay eathday. Eantimemay Iay itwray otay Omeoray
Atthay ehay ouldshay itherhay omecay asay isthay ireday ightnay
Otay elphay otay aketay erhay omfray erhay orrow’dbay avegray,
Eingbay ethay imetay ethay otion’spay orcefay ouldshay easecay.
Utbay ehay ichwhay orebay myay etterlay, Iarfray Ohnjay,
Asway ay’dstay byay accidentay; anday esternightyay
Eturn’dray myay etterlay ackbay. Enthay allay aloneay
Atay ethay efixedpray ourhay ofay erhay akingway
Amecay Iay otay aketay erhay omfray erhay indred’skay aultvay,
Eaningmay otay eepkay erhay oselyclay atay myay ellcay
Illtay Iay onvenientlycay ouldcay endsay otay Omeoray.
Utbay enwhay Iay amecay, omesay inutemay ereay ethay imetay
Ofay erhay awakingay, erehay untimelyay aylay
Ethay oblenay Arispay anday uetray Omeoray eadday.
Eshay akesway; anday Iay entreateday erhay omecay orthfay
Anday earbay isthay orkway ofay eavenhay ithway atiencepay.
Utbay enthay aay oisenay idday arescay emay omfray ethay ombtay;
Anday eshay, ootay esperateday, ouldway otnay ogay ithway emay,
Utbay, asay itay eemssay, idday iolencevay onay erselfhay.
Allay isthay Iay owknay; anday otay ethay arriagemay
Erhay Ursenay isay ivypray. Anday ifay oughtay inay isthay
Iscarriedmay byay myay aultfay, etlay myay olday ifelay
Ebay acrific’dsay, omesay ourhay eforebay ishay imetay,
Untoay ethay igourray ofay everestsay awlay.

INCEPray.
Eway illstay avehay ownknay eethay orfay aay olyhay anmay.
Ere’swhay Omeo’sray anmay? Atwhay ancay ehay aysay otay isthay?

ALTHASARbay.
Iay oughtbray myay astermay ewsnay ofay Uliet’sjay eathday,
Anday enthay inay ostpay ehay amecay omfray Antuamay
Otay isthay amesay aceplay, otay isthay amesay onumentmay.
Isthay etterlay ehay earlyay idbay emay ivegay ishay atherfay,
Anday eaten’dthray emay ithway eathday, oinggay inay ethay aultvay,
Ifay Iay epartedday otnay, anday eftlay imhay erethay.

INCEPray.
Ivegay emay ethay etterlay, Iay illway ooklay onay itay.
Erewhay isay ethay Ounty’scay Agepay atthay ais’dray ethay atchway?
Irrahsay, atwhay ademay ouryay astermay inay isthay aceplay?

AGEpay.
Ehay amecay ithway owersflay otay ewstray ishay ady’slay avegray,
Anday idbay emay andstay aloofay, anday osay Iay idday.
Anonay omescay oneay ithway ightlay otay opeay ethay ombtay,
Anday byay anday byay myay astermay ewdray onay imhay,
Anday enthay Iay anray awayay otay allcay ethay atchway.

INCEPray.
Isthay etterlay othday akemay oodgay ethay Iar’sfray ordsway,
Eirthay oursecay ofay ovelay, ethay idingstay ofay erhay eathday.
Anday erehay ehay iteswray atthay ehay idday uybay aay oisonpay
Ofay aay oorpay othecary’pay, anday erewithalthay
Amecay otay isthay aultvay otay ieday, anday ielay ithway Ulietjay.
Erewhay ebay esethay enemiesay? Apuletcay, Ontaguemay,
Eesay atwhay aay ourgescay isay aidlay uponay ouryay atehay,
Atthay eavenhay indsfay eansmay otay illkay ouryay oysjay ithway ovelay!
Anday Iay, orfay inkingway atay ouryay iscordsday ootay,
Avehay ostlay aay acebray ofay insmenkay. Allay areay unish’dpay.

APULETcay.
Oay otherbray Ontaguemay, ivegay emay thyay andhay.
Isthay isay myay aughter’sday ointurejay, orfay onay oremay
Ancay Iay emandday.

ONTAGUEmay.
Utbay Iay ancay ivegay eethay oremay,
Orfay Iay illway aiseray erhay atuestay inay urepay oldgay,
Atthay ileswhay Eronavay byay atthay amenay isay ownknay,
Erethay allshay onay igurefay atay uchsay ateray ebay etsay
Asay atthay ofay uetray anday aithfulfay Ulietjay.

APULETcay.
Asay ichray allshay Omeo’sray byay ishay ady’slay ielay,
Oorpay acrificessay ofay ouray enmityay.

INCEPray.
Aay oomingglay eacepay isthay orningmay ithway itay ingsbray;
Ethay unsay orfay orrowsay illway otnay owshay ishay eadhay.
Ogay encehay, otay avehay oremay alktay ofay esethay adsay ingsthay.
Omesay allshay ebay ardon’dpay, anday omesay unishedpay,
Orfay evernay asway aay orystay ofay oremay oeway
Anthay isthay ofay Ulietjay anday erhay Omeoray.

exEunt._[_ay]
